Question #1 (ID: 473941)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2000-2001, 2020-2021, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 15^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{3}-2[/math]
খ. [math]2-\sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]1+\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3-\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2-\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan 15^{\circ}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\tan 30^{\circ}}{1+\tan 30^{\circ}}=\frac{1-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}{1+1 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}=2-\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #2 (ID: 473943)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2004-2005, 1999-2000, 2015-2016, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2010-2011, 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Barishal, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jagannath University (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin75^{\circ}+\sin15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)=\tan 60^{\circ}=\sqrt{3}\\\text{}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #3 (ID: 473944)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=x[/math] হলে, [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math] এর মান কত? [math](I f \tan \theta+\sec \theta=x[/math] Than what is the value of [math]\operatorname{cose} \theta ?)[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1-x^{2}}{1+x^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে,[math]\operatorname{sec} \theta+\tan \theta=x-(\mathrm{i})[/math]
সুতরাং, [math]\operatorname{sec} \theta-\operatorname{tan} \theta=\frac{1}{X}-(\mathrm{ii})[/math]
এখন, i ও ii বিয়োগ করলে[math]2 \tan \theta=x-\frac{1}{x}[/math]
বা, [math]2 \tan \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x}[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{\operatorname{tan} \theta} \cdot \frac{1}{\operatorname{Cos} \theta}=\frac{2 x}{x^{1}-1}[/math]
বা, [math]\operatorname{Cot}^{2} \theta=\frac{x^{2}}{\left(x^{2}-1\right)^{2}}[/math]
বা, [math]\operatorname{Cosec}^{2} \theta-1=\frac{4 x^{2}}{\left(x^{2}-1\right)^{2}}[/math]
বা, [math]\operatorname{Cosec}^{2} \theta=\frac{4 x^{2}}{\left(x^{2}-1\right)}+1[/math]
বা, [math]=\left(\frac{a x^{2}+\left(x^{2}-1\right)}{\left(x^{2}-1\right)^{2}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]=\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]


Explanation:
এখানে একটি সহজ অনুসিদ্ধান্ত ব্যাবহার করা হয়েছে। যা হল, [math](\operatorname{sec} \theta+\sec \theta)(\operatorname{sec} \theta-\tan \theta)=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore(\tan \theta+\sec \theta)=\frac{1}{\tan \theta-\sec \theta}[/math]


Sub-Questions:

Question #4 (ID: 473945)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021-2022, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে যদি [math]a=3, b=3 \sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]A=30^{\circ}[/math] হয় তবে B ও C এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]45^{\circ}, 30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]30^{\circ}, 40^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]20^{\circ}, 45^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]10^{\circ}, 70^{\circ}[/math]
ঙ. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: E.[math]30^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{3 \sqrt{3} \times \sin 30^{\circ}}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=60^{\circ} \text { or } 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=0^{\circ} \text { or }\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-120^{\circ}-30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #5 (ID: 473947)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\cos \alpha+\sin \beta=0, \sin \alpha-\cos \beta=1[/math] এবং [math]90^{\circ} \leq\{\alpha, \beta\} \leq 180^{\circ}[/math] হয়, তবে [math](\alpha-\beta)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]75^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]30^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
[math](\cos \alpha+\sin \beta)^{2}+(\sin \alpha-\cos \beta)^{2}=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+1+2 \cos \alpha \sin \beta-2 \sin \alpha \cos \beta=1 \\\Rightarrow(\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\cos \alpha \sin \beta)=\frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin (\alpha-\beta)=\sin 30^{\circ} \therefore \alpha-\beta=30^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #6 (ID: 473948)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 2 \theta \tan \theta=1[/math] সমীকরণে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]n \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]n \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
C. [math]2 n \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
D. [math]2 n \pi-\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]n \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=y \Rightarrow \frac{2 y}{1-y^{2}} \cdot y=1 ; 2 y^{2}=1-y^{2} \quad \therefore 3 y^{2}=1 \quad y=\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \quad \theta=n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{6} \text { But, first option is the first choice. }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #7 (ID: 473949)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের তিনটি শীর্ষবিন্দু [math]\mathrm{A}(5,12), \mathrm{B}(-12,5)[/math] এবং [math]C(-7,17)[/math] হলে [math]\angle A C B[/math] কোণের মান হবে-

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]A B=c=13 \sqrt{2} ; B C=a=13 ; A C=b=13[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos C=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 b a}=0 \therefore \angle C=\angle A C B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #8 (ID: 473950)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos 2 \theta=\frac{24}{25}[/math] হলে, [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\pm 7[/math]
B. [math]\pm \frac{5}{7}[/math]
C. [math]\pm \frac{1}{7}[/math]
D. [math]\pm \frac{7}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\pm \frac{1}{7}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 \theta=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{24}{25} \quad \therefore \tan \theta= \pm \frac{1}{7}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #9 (ID: 473951)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014, 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]9, 40[/math] ও [math]41[/math] একক বাহুবিশিষ্ট একটি ত্রিভুজের পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস কত?

Options:
ক. [math]41[/math]
খ. [math]21.5[/math]
গ. [math]20.5[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{9 \times 40 \times 41}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]41[/math]

Solution:
[math]s=\frac{9+40+41}{2}=45[/math]
 [math]\therefore \Delta=\sqrt{45(45-9)(45-40)(45-41)}=180[/math]
পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস, [math]=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]=2 \times \frac{\mathrm{abc}}{4 \Delta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{abc}}{2 \Delta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \times 40 \times 41}{2 \times 180}[/math]
 [math]=41[/math]
 এককপরিবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ, [math]R=20.5[/math]


Explanation:

Question #10 (ID: 473953)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan x+\tan 2 x+\tan 3 x=\tan x \tan 2 x \tan 3 x[/math] - সমীকরণে x এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{12}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{n \pi}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan x+\tan 2 x+\tan 3 x=\tan x \tan 2 x \tan 3 x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan x+\tan 2 x=-\tan 3 x(1-\tan x \tan 2 x)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan x+\tan 2 x}{1-\tan x \tan 2 x}=-\tan 3 x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan 3 x=-\tan 3 x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \tan 3 x=0 \Rightarrow \tan 3 x=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 x=n \pi \Rightarrow x=\frac{n \pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\text { Shortcut: Use Calculator }[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #11 (ID: 473954)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013, 2006-2007 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]3 \sec ^{4} \theta+8=10 \sec ^{2} \theta[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
B. [math]\pm 1[/math]
C. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}, \pm 1[/math]
D. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}, \pm 1[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}, \pm 1[/math]

Solution:
[math]3 \sec ^{4} \theta+8-10 \sec ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)^{2}+8-10-10 \tan ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3+6 \tan ^{2} \theta+3 \tan ^{4} \theta-2-10 \tan ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{4} \theta-3 \tan ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)-1\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(3 \tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=[/math]
 [math]\pm 1, \tan \theta=[/math]
 [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #12 (ID: 473955)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলি [math]2 x+3, x^{2}+3 x+3[/math] হলে, বৃহত্ত কোণটি হবে-

Options:
ক. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]180^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]120^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
সবচেয়ে বড় বাহু [math]a=\left(x^{2}+3 x+3\right)[/math]
 এবং বড় কোণ A[math]\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(2 x+3)^{2}+\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)^{2}-\left(x^{2}+3 x+3\right)^{2}}{2 \times(2 x+3)\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}=\cos 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #13 (ID: 473957)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011, 2022-2023, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]60^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #14 (ID: 473958)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: Engg Guccho (Ka Unit – Without Architecture)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\Delta[/math]ABC তে BC = a = 3cm [math]CA = bcm , AB = c = 4cm এবং \angle B = 60^\circ[/math] হলে b এবং [math]\angle[/math]A এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]18 \mathrm{~cm}, 74^{\circ} 9^{\prime} 15^{\prime \prime}[/math]
B. [math]3.6 \mathrm{~cm}, 46^{\circ} 13^{\prime} 11^{\prime \prime}[/math]
C. [math]165 \mathrm{~cm}, 35^{\circ} 10^{\prime}[/math]
D. [math]18 \mathrm{~cm}, 70^{\circ} 30^{\prime}[/math]
E. [math]64 \mathrm{~cm}, 78^{\circ} 10^{\prime}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]3.6 \mathrm{~cm}, 46^{\circ} 13^{\prime} 11^{\prime \prime}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}}{2 a c}=\cos B \Rightarrow \frac{4^{2}+3^{2}-b^{2}}{2 \times 4 \times 3}=\cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2} \\25-b^{2}=12 \Rightarrow b^{2}=25-12=13 \Rightarrow b=3.6 \mathrm{~cm}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\cos A=\frac{(3.6)^{2}+4^{2}-3^{2}}{2 \times 3.6 \times 4}=\frac{499}{720} \Rightarrow A=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{499}{720}\right)=46^{\circ} 13^{\prime}a[/math]


Explanation:

Question #15 (ID: 473959)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Engg Guccho (Ka Unit – Without Architecture)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\frac{2 \sin \alpha}{1+\sin u+\cos \alpha}=\lambda[/math] হয় তাহলে [math]\frac{1+\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha}[/math] এর মান হল-

Options:
A. [math]-\lambda[/math]
B. [math]\lambda[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{\lambda}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{-1}{\lambda}[/math]
E. [math]\text { None of them }[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\lambda[/math]

Solution:
[math]\lambda=\frac{2 \sin \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha }[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \times \frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha }{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\pi}{2}}}{1+\frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha }{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha }{2}}+\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\mathrm{\alpha }}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\mathrm{\alpha }}{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4 \tan \frac{\alpha }{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\mathrm{u}}{2}+2 \tan \frac{\mathrm{\alpha }}{2}+1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\mathrm{\alpha }}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \frac{\mathrm{\alpha }}{2}}{\tan ^{\frac{\alpha }{2}}+2}[/math]
 [math]\text { Again, } \frac{1+\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}-\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}}{1+\frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha }{2}+2 \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}-1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{1}{2}+2 \tan \frac{\alpha }{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \frac{a}{2}\left(1+\tan ^{\frac{\alpha }{2}}\right)}{\left(1+\tan \frac{\alpha }{2}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha }{3}}{1+\tan \frac{\alpha }{2}}=\lambda[/math]
 [math]\text { Alternate: Given, } \frac{2 \sin \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\lambda ; \text { Let, } \frac{1+\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha}=x[/math]
 [math]\frac{\lambda}{x}=\frac{2 \sin \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha+\cos \alpha} \times \frac{1+\sin \alpha}{1+\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin \alpha(1+\sin \alpha)}{(1+\sin \alpha)^{2}-\cos ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin \alpha(1+\sin \alpha)}{1+2 \sin \alpha+\sin ^{2} \alpha-\cos ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{2 \sin a(1+\sin \alpha)}{2 \sin \alpha+2 \sin ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin a(1+\sin \alpha)}{2 \sin a(1+\sin \alpha)}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\lambda[/math]


Explanation:

Question #16 (ID: 473960)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: General and Science Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A - B = \frac{\pi}{4}[/math] হলে [math](1 + \tan A)(1 - \tan B)[/math] এর মান

Options:
A. [math]-2[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
D. [math]-\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan(A - B) = \frac{\tan A - \tan B}{1 + \tan A \tan B}[/math]
; সেখান থেকে [math]AB[/math]
 এর মান বের করে গুণফল নির্ণয় করলে ফলাফল [math]-2[/math]

Question #17 (ID: 473961)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: General and Science Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan(\sin^{-1}(\sqrt{1 - x^2})) = \sin(\cos^{-1} \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}})[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এর মান

Options:
A. [math]\pm\sqrt{5}/3[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{5}/3[/math]
C. [math]-\sqrt{5}/3[/math]
D. [math]5/3[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
উভয় পাশে কোণের সমানুপাতিক মান তুলনা করে [math]x = \pm\sqrt{5}/3[/math]

Question:
[math]\theta=\cos \frac{1}{5}[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\left(1-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{16}{25}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{9}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{8}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\theta=\cos \frac{14}{5} \Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\frac{\left(1-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}=\cos 2 \theta-2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\\=2 \times \frac{16}{25}-1=\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Question #19 (ID: 473963)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023 | Boards:  | Tags: General and Science Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)+\sin \left(\alpha+\frac{5 \pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-1[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]-\cos \alpha[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3} \sin \alpha[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin \left(\alpha+\frac{5 \pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin \left(\alpha+\pi-\frac{5 \pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin \left\{\pi+\left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]-\sin \left(\alpha-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan A \cdot \tan B = 1[/math] হলে [math]A + B[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
যখন [math]\tan A \cdot \tan B = 1[/math]
, তখন [math]A + B = \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 হয়, কারণ [math]\tan(A+B)[/math]
 তখন অসীম হয়। এটি ত্রিকোণমিতির একটি মৌলিক নিয়ম।

Question #21 (ID: 473966)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Textiles
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan x \tan 2x = 1[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]n\pi[/math]
খ. [math]n\pi \pm \dfrac{\pi}{6}[/math]
গ. [math]2n\pi \pm \dfrac{\pi}{6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]2n\pi - \dfrac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan x \tan 2x = 1 \Rightarrow \tan 2x = \cot x[/math]
। আবার, [math]\cot x = \tan\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2} - x\right)[/math]
। অতএব, [math]2x = \dfrac{\pi}{2} - x + n\pi[/math]
 ⇒ [math]x = \dfrac{\pi}{6} + n\pi[/math]
 অথবা [math]x = -\dfrac{\pi}{6} + n\pi[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{5}{12}[/math] এবং [math]\theta[/math] সূক্ষ্মকোণ হলে [math]\sin \theta+\sec (-\theta)[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{21}{156}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{229}{156}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{219}{156}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{17}{32}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{229}{156}[/math]

Solution:
পার্শ্বের ত্রিভুজ হতে পাই
[Image]
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{5}{13}[/math]
 এবং [math]\sec \theta=\frac{13}{12}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta+\sec (-\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \theta+\sec \theta=\frac{5}{13}+\frac{13}{12}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{229}{156}[/math]

Question #23 (ID: 473936)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cot A-\tan A[/math] সমান-

Options:
A. [math]2 \tan 2 A[/math]
B. [math]2 \cot 2 A[/math]
C. [math]2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}[/math]
D. [math]2 \sin ^{2} A[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2 \cot 2 A[/math]

Solution:
[math]\text { LHS }=\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}-\frac{\sin A}{\sin A}=\frac{\cos ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} A}{\sin A \cos A}[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos 2 A / \sin 2 A=2 \cot 2 A[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sin 780^{\circ} \cdot \cos 390^{\circ}-\sin 330^{\circ} \cdot \cos \left(-300^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-1[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin 780^{\circ} \cos 390^{\circ}-\sin 330^{\circ} \cos 300^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin 60^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}-\left(-\cos 60^{\circ}\right) \sin 30^{\circ}=\sin \left(60^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)=\sin 90^{\circ}=1[/math]

[math]\tan 40^{\circ} \tan 50^{\circ} \tan 60^{\circ}[/math] এর মান-

D. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:

 [math]=\tan 40^{\circ} \tan \left(90^{\circ}-40^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cot 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]

Question #28 (ID: 473909)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


[math]sin B = x[/math] হলে [math]sinC[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]x[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{x}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{x^{2}-1}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{1-x^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\sqrt{1-x^{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin B=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(180^{\circ}-\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(180^{\circ}-90^{\circ}-C\right)[/math]
 [math]=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos C=x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{x}^{2} \Rightarrow 1-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{x}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \mathrm{C}=\sqrt{1-\mathrm{x}^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #29 (ID: 473910)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit)

Question:
একটি ত্রিভূজের a, b, c তিনটি বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে 3, 5, 7 হলে, [math]\angle C = ?[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]120^\circ[/math]
খ. [math]\cos^{-1}\left(\frac{11}{14}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\cos^{-1}\left(\frac{13}{14}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sin^{-1}\left(\frac{11}{14}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
কসমাস সূত্র প্রয়োগে, [math]\cos C = \frac{3^2 + 5^2 - 7^2}{2 \cdot 3 \cdot 5} = -\frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow C = 120^\circ[/math]

Explanation:

Question #30 (ID: 473911)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\operatorname{cosec} 10^{\circ}-4 \sin 70^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]-2[/math]
D. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\operatorname{cosec} 10^{\circ}-4 \sin 70^{\circ}=\frac{1}{\sin 10^{\circ}}-4 \sin 70^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1-4 \sin 70^{\circ} \sin 10^{\circ}}{\sin 10^{\circ}}=\frac{1-2\left(\cos 60^{\circ}-\cos 80^{\circ}\right)}{\sin \left(90^{\circ}-80^{\circ}\right)} \\=\frac{1-2\left(\frac{1}{2}-\cos 80^{\circ}\right)}{\cos 80^{\circ}}=\frac{1-1+2 \cos 80^{\circ}}{\cos 80^{\circ}}=2\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Solution:

Question #33 (ID: 473915)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit)

Question:
[math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. sin(A - B)
B. sin(B-A)
C. 1
D. 0


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}[/math]
 [math]=-\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=\sin (B-A)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #34 (ID: 473916)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018, 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Rajshahi (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. sin (A - B)
B. sin(B - A)
C. cos(B - A)
D. -cos(A-B)


Correct Answer: B.sin(B - A)

Solution:
$\begin{array}{l}=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B)=-\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \sin (A-B) \\=-\sin (A-B)=\sin (B-A)\end{array}$[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}[/math]
 [math]=-\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-[/math]
 [math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (A-B)=\sin (B-A)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #40 (ID: 473924)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\sin \alpha-\sin \beta=2[/math] এবং [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=3[/math] হলে, [math]\cos (\alpha-\beta)[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{8}{13}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4}{13}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{9}{13}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \alpha-\sin \beta[/math]
 [math]=2 \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=3 \ldots \ldots . \text { (ii) }[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \div \text { (ii) } \Rightarrow \frac{\sin \alpha-\sin \beta}{\cos \alpha+\cos \beta}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \sin \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}{2 \cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{4}{9}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{.2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9-4}{9+4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos (\alpha-\beta)=\frac{5}{13}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
যদি [math]\tan \left(\frac{\theta}{2}\right)=\frac{3}{4}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{9}{16}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{24}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{25}{7}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}=\frac{1-\frac{9}{16}}{1+\frac{9}{16}}=\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Question #44 (ID: 473930)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}=\cos[/math]
 [math]\left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

 [math]+\sin \left\{7 \times 90^{\circ}-198^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan \left\{180^{\circ}-12^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 198^{\circ}-\cos 198^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}-\tan 12=0[/math]

Question:

[Image]


[math]b = 3[/math] একক হলে [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল কত বর্গ একক?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{9}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C} \\\therefore c=\frac{3 \times \sin 30^{\circ}}{\sin 120^{\circ}}=\frac{3}{2} \times \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}=\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} b c \sin A=\frac{1}{2} \times 3 \times \sqrt{3} \times \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 বর্গ একক

 [math]\cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

Options:
A. [math]6 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
B. [math]4 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
C. [math]3 \sqrt{3} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
D. [math]2 \sqrt{3} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]3 \sqrt{3} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\angle \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-[/math]
 [math]\angle \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]-\angle \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-90^{\circ}-60^{\circ}=[/math]
30^{\circ}$ত্রিভুজের সাইন সূত্র অনুসারে, [math]\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b=[/math]
 [math]\frac{3 \times \sin 60^{\circ}}{\sin 30^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore b[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 \times \sqrt{3}}{2 \times \frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=3 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #68 (ID: 473887)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\sin \frac{A}{2}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{\frac{2}{5}}[/math]
খ. [math]-\sqrt{\frac{2}{5}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2}{5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]-\frac{2}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\sqrt{\frac{2}{5}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]s=\frac{7+6+5}{2}=9[/math]
 [math]\sin \frac{A}{2}=\sqrt{\frac{(s-b)(s-c)}{b c}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{(9-6)(9-5)}{6 \times 5}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{3 \times 4}{6 \times 5}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{2}{5}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #69 (ID: 473873)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}, \sin B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে [math]\tan (A+B)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1-\sqrt{2}}{1+\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1+\sqrt{2}}{1-\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{2}-1}{\sqrt{2}+1}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{2}+1}{\sqrt{2}-1}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \quad \therefore A=45^{\circ}[/math]
আবার, [math]\sin B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\tan \left(45^{\circ}+B\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan B}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \tan B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}{1-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{2}+1}{\sqrt{2}-1}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{\sin (\alpha+\beta)-\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\cos (\alpha-\beta)-\cos (\alpha+\beta)}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\cot \alpha[/math]
B. [math]\cot \beta[/math]
C. [math]\tan \alpha[/math]
D. [math]\tan \beta[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin (\alpha+\beta)-\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\cos (\alpha-\beta)-\cos (\alpha+\beta)}=\frac{2 \cos \alpha \sin \beta}{2 \sin \alpha \sin \beta}=\cot \alpha[/math]

 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin 10^{\circ} \cos 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} 10^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{p}[/math]
 [math]=2 \mathrm{p} \sqrt{1-\mathrm{p}^{2}}[/math]

Question #72 (ID: 473876)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 2 \theta-\tan \theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]\operatorname{cosec} 2 \theta[/math]
B. [math]\tan \theta \cos \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\tan \theta \sec 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan 2 \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 2 \theta}{\cos 2 \theta}-\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 2 \theta \cdot \cos \theta-\cos 2 \theta \cdot \sin \theta}{\cos 2 \theta \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{\sin (2 \theta-\theta)}{\cos 2 \theta \cos \theta}=[/math]
 [math]\sec 2 \theta \tan \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #73 (ID: 473877)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \beta=\frac{q}{p}[/math] হলে [math]\cos 2 \beta[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2 p q}{p^{2}-q^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2 p q}{p^{2}+q^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{p^{2}-q^{2}}{p^{2}+q^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{p^{2}+q^{2}}{p^{2}-q^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{p^{2}-q^{2}}{p^{2}+q^{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 \beta=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \beta}{1+\tan ^{2} \beta}=\frac{1-\frac{q^{2}}{p^{2}}}{1+\frac{q^{2}}{p^{2}}}=\frac{p^{2}-q^{2}}{p^{2}+q^{2}}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #74 (ID: 473878)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{8}\right)[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2 + \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2 - \sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{4} \sqrt{2 + \sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{4} \sqrt{2 - \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos \frac{\pi}{8}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{2+2 \times \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #75 (ID: 473879)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A+B+C=\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\operatorname{cosec}(B+C)[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]-\sec A[/math]
B. [math]\sec \mathrm{A}[/math]
C. [math]-\operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{A}[/math]
D. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{A}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]-\sec A[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}A+B+C=\frac{3 \pi}{2} \Rightarrow B+C=\frac{3 \pi}{2}-A \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec}(B+C)=\operatorname{cosec}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}-A\right) \\\therefore \operatorname{cosec}(B+C)=-\sec A\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]\angle \mathrm{C}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{39}{12}\right)[/math]
খ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{12}{39}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(-\frac{1}{4}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos C=\frac{4^{2}+6^{2}-8^{2}}{2 \times 4 \times 6}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-12}{48}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{-1}{4}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #85 (ID: 473859)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board

Question:
[math]\cos 2 A=\frac{3}{5}[/math] , sin Aএর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{10}}[/math]
B. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]
C. [math]\pm \sqrt{\frac{3}{5}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}=\frac{3}{5}\\\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin ^{2} A=\frac{3}{5}\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} A=1-\frac{3}{5}\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\frac{5-3}{5}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\frac{2}{10}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} A=\frac{1}{5}\\\therefore \sin A= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #86 (ID: 473860)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cot \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] , [math]\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] হলে sec [math]\theta[/math] -এর মান কত

Options:
A. [math]\frac{-5}{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{-5}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{ } \cot \theta=\frac{3}{4}\\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{4}{3}\\\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta=\left(\frac{4}{3}\right)^{2}\\\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta-1=\frac{16}{9}\\\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=\frac{16}{9}+1\\\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=\frac{25}{9}\\\Rightarrow \sec \theta= \pm \frac{5}{3} \text{}\end{array}[/math]
যেহেতু, cot [math]\theta[/math]
 ধনাত্মক এবং [math]\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
 সুতরাং, [math]\theta[/math]
 এর অবস্থান হবে তৃতীয় চতুর্ভাগে। তৃতীয় চতুর্ভাগে sec [math]\theta[/math]
 ঋণাত্মক।[math]\therefore \sec \theta=-\frac{5}{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #87 (ID: 473861)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math] হলে sin 2 [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 2 \theta=\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{2 \cdot \frac{1}{2}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}}=\frac{1}{1+\frac{1}{4}}=\frac{1}{\frac{4+1}{4}}=\frac{4}{5}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sin (A-B)[/math]
B. [math]\sin (B-A)[/math]
C. [math]\cos (A-B)[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
এখানে, [math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=-\left(\cos ^{2} B-\cos ^{2} A\right) \\=-\sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)\end{array}[/math]
 [সূত্র হতে][math]=-\sin \frac{\pi}{2} \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=-\sin (A-B) \\=\sin (B-A)\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #89 (ID: 473863)

Question:
[math]\frac{1-\tan 25^{\circ}}{1+\tan 25^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান নিম্নের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\cot 20^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]\tan 20^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]\tan 70^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\cot 70^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1-\tan 25^{\circ}}{1+\tan 25^{\circ}}=\frac{\tan 45^{\circ}-\tan 25^{\circ}}{1+\tan 45^{\circ} \tan 25^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(45^{\circ}-25^{\circ}\right)\left[\because \tan (A-B)=\frac{\tan A-\tan B}{1+\tan A \tan B}\right][/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ}[/math]

Question #90 (ID: 473864)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math] তবে [math]\cos 3 \theta[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{8}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{3}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3}{2}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \cos 3 \theta & =4 \cos ^{3} \theta-3 \cos \theta \\& =4\left\{\frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\}^{-3}-3 \cdot \frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \\& =4 \cdot \frac{1}{8}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}-\frac{3}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \\& =\frac{1}{2}\left\{\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}-3\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\} \\& =\frac{1}{2}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:

 [সূত্র হতে][math]=2 p \sqrt{1-p^{2}}[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে]

Question:
[math]\frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\cot 70^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}& \frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\cot 70^{\circ}} \\= & \frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\tan \left(90^{\circ}-54^{\circ}\right)}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\cot \left(90^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right)} \\= & \frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\cot 54^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\tan 20^{\circ}} \\= & 1+1=2\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #95 (ID: 473869)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি , [math]\cos \theta=\frac{12}{13}[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{25}{144}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{5}{12}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{13}{12}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{12}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
আমরা জানি যে [math]\sin^2 \theta + \cos^2 \theta = 1[/math]
।এখন,[math]\cos \theta = \frac{12}{13} \Rightarrow \cos^2 \theta = \left(\frac{12}{13}\right)^2 = \frac{144}{169}[/math]
সুতরাং,[math]\sin^2 \theta = 1 - \cos^2 \theta = 1 - \frac{144}{169} = \frac{169 - 144}{169} = \frac{25}{169}[/math]
এখন, [math]\sin \theta = \sqrt{\frac{25}{169}} = \frac{5}{13}[/math]
 (কারণ [math]0 < \theta < \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 হওয়ায় [math]\sin \theta[/math]
 ধনাত্মক হবে)।তাহলে,[math]\tan \theta = \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta} = \frac{\frac{5}{13}}{\frac{12}{13}} = \frac{5}{12}[/math]
অতএব, [math]\tan \theta = \frac{5}{12}[/math]
।

Explanation:

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\angle A: \angle B: \angle C=1: 2: 3[/math] হলে [math]a: b: c=[/math]কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]2: \sqrt{3}: 1[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{3}: 2: 1[/math]
গ. [math]2: 3: 1[/math]
ঘ. [math]1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\angle A=\frac{1}{1+2+3} \times 180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{180^{\circ}}{6}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\angle \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=60^{\circ}[/math]
 এবং [math]\angle \mathrm{C}=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore a: b: c=[/math]
 [math]\sin A: \sin \mathrm{B}:[/math]
 [math]\sin C[/math]
 [math]=\sin 30^{\circ}: \sin 60^{\circ}:[/math]
 [math]\sin 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}: \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}: 1=1:[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{3}: 2[/math]

Question #100 (ID: 473855)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\angle A=60^{\circ}, b=2[/math] এবং [math]c = 4[/math] হলে, [math]a[/math]-এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{bc}} \\\Rightarrow \cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{2^{2}+4^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2.2 .4} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}=\frac{20-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{16} \Rightarrow 20-\mathrm{a}^{2}=8 \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{a}^{2}=12 \therefore \mathrm{a}=2 \sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]

Question #102 (ID: 473836)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board

Question:
[math]\sin 65^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos 40^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sin 20^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \sin 40^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin 65^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin 65^{\circ}+\cos \left(90^{\circ}-25^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin 65^{\circ}+\sin 25^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{65^{\circ}+25^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{65^{\circ}-25^{\circ}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]

Question #104 (ID: 473838)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\operatorname{cos} 15^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos 15^{\circ} =[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(45^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin 15^{0}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}} \cos 15^{0}=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}} \\\sin 75^{0}=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}} \cos 75^{0}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}} \\\tan 75^{0}=2+\sqrt{3} \tan 15^{0}=2-\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]

Question #105 (ID: 473839)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\cot 70^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cot 54^{\circ}}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 20^{\circ}}{\cot 70^{\circ}} \\=\frac{\cot \left(90^{\circ}-36^{\circ}\right)}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan \left(90^{\circ}-70^{\circ}\right)}{\cot 70^{\circ}} \\=\frac{\tan 36^{\circ}}{\tan 36^{\circ}}+\frac{\cot 70^{\circ}}{\cot 70^{\circ}}=1+1=2\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{\sin \left(45^{\circ}+A\right)+\sin \left(45^{\circ}-A\right)}{\cos \left(45^{\circ}-A\right)-\cos \left(45^{\circ}+A\right)}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\cot A[/math]
B. [math]-1[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\tan A[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin \left(45^{\circ}+A\right)+\sin \left(45^{\circ}-A\right)}{\cos \left(45^{\circ}-A\right)-\cos \left(45^{\circ}+A\right)} \\=\frac{2 \sin 45^{\circ} \cos A}{2 \sin 45^{\circ} \sin A}=\cot A\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #107 (ID: 473841)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin 2 \theta=\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{2 \times \frac{1}{2}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}}=\frac{1}{1+\frac{1}{4}}=\frac{4}{5}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #108 (ID: 473842)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \frac{\alpha}{2}=7[/math] হলে, [math]4 \sin \alpha-3 \cos \alpha=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]5[/math]
B. [math]4[/math]
C. [math]3[/math]
D. [math]6[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]4 \sin \alpha-3 \cos \alpha[/math]
 [math]=4 \cdot \sin 2 \cdot \frac{\alpha}{2}-3[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos 2 \cdot \frac{\alpha}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow4 \cdot \frac{2 \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}-3[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow4[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{2 \times 7}{1+7^{2}}[/math]
 [math]-3 \times \frac{1-7^{2}}{1+7^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{56}{50}+\frac{144}{50}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{200}{50}=4[/math]


Explanation:

Question #109 (ID: 473843)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{8}\right)[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]1-\sqrt{2}[/math]
B. [math]-1+\sqrt{2}[/math]
C. [math]1+\sqrt{2}[/math]
D. [math]-1-\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\tan \frac{\pi}{8}=\frac{\sin \frac{\pi}{8}}{\cos \frac{\pi}{8}}=\frac{2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}{2 \sin \frac{\pi}{8} \cos \frac{\pi}{8}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \frac{\pi}{4}}{\sin \frac{\pi}{4}}=\operatorname{cosec} \frac{\pi}{4}-\cot \frac{\pi}{4}=\sqrt{2}-1\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{1-\tan ^{2}\left(45^{\circ}+x\right)}{1+\tan ^{2}\left(45^{\circ}+x\right)}[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

B. [math]\sin 2 x[/math]

D. [math]\cos 2 x[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

 [math]=\cos 2[/math]
 [math]\left(45^{\circ}+x\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(90^{\circ}+2 x\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin 2 x[/math]

Question #111 (ID: 473845)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos 2 A=\frac{3}{5}[/math] হলে [math]\sin \mathrm{A}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{10}}[/math]
B. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]
C. [math]\pm \sqrt{\frac{3}{5}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-\frac{3}{5}=2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\frac{2}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}=\frac{1}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \mathrm{A}= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #112 (ID: 473846)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board

Question:
যদি [math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math] হয় তবে [math]\cos 3 \theta[/math] এর মান -

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{4}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}\left(a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}\right)[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{4}\left(a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos 3 \theta=4 \cos ^{3} \theta-3 \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4\left\{\frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\}^{3}-3[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{1}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{4}{8}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [math]-\frac{3}{2}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left\{\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 6 \times 8 \times \sin 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 48 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=12 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 বর্গ একক

Question:
যে কোনো ত্রিভুজ ABC এর ক্ষেত্রে নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

খ. [math]b = c sin A + a sin C[/math]
গ. [math]\Delta=\frac{1}{2} a b \cos C[/math]
ঘ. [math]\cos A=\frac{\left(b^{2}+c^{2}+a^{2}\right)}{(2 b c)}[/math]

-এর ক্ষেত্রে,[math]\begin{array}{l}a=b \cos C+c \cos B \\b=a \cos C+c \cos A \\c=a \cos B+b \cos A\end{array}[/math]

Question #115 (ID: 473849)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]10[/math] একক। যদি, [math]c=10 \sqrt{3}[/math] একক হয়, তবে [math]C[/math] কোণের মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
পরিব্যাসার্ধ R হলে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{10 \sqrt{3}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \times 10\Rightarrow \sin \mathrm{C}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin 60^{\circ} \therefore \mathrm{C}=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #116 (ID: 473850)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রে [math]c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}-c a=0[/math] হলে [math]\angle \mathrm{B}[/math] এর পরিমাণ—

Options:
A. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}-c a=0\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}=\mathrm{ca} \Rightarrow\frac{\mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ca}}=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos B=\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ} \therefore \angle B=60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #117 (ID: 473851)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এ [math]\cos \mathrm{A}=\sin \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{C}[/math] হলে, [math]\angle \mathbf{A}[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos A+\cos C=\sin B\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=\sin B\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right) \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}=\sin 2 \cdot \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}=\mathrm{B} \Rightarrow \mathrm{A}=\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}\\\Rightarrow 2 A=A+B+C=\pi \quad \therefore A=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #119 (ID: 473853)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\sqrt{3}[/math] হলে-

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i.} \quad \sin 2 \theta =\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\\\text{ii.} \cos 2 \theta=\frac{1}{2}\\\text{iii.} \tan 2 \theta=-\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\sqrt{3}=\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\text{(i) } \sin 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(2 \times 60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{.2}[/math]
 [math]\text{(ii) } \cos 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(2 \times 60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\text{(iii) } \tan 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(2 \times 60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=-\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \text { (ii) }[/math]
 নং তথ্যটি সঠিক নয়

Explanation:

Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলোর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে 3, 5, 7 একক হলে,

i. ত্রিভুজটির পরিসীমা [math]15[/math] একক

ii. ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{15}{2} \sqrt{3}[/math] বর্গ একক

iii. ত্রিভুজটির বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]120^{\circ}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
(i) পরিসীমা [math]=3+5+7=15[/math]
 একক(ii) ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\sqrt{7.5(7.5-3)(7.5-5)(7.5-7)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 বর্গ একক[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { (iii) } \cos C=\frac{3^{2}+5^{2}-7^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5}=-\frac{1}{2}=\cos 120^{\circ} \\\therefore C=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Question #123 (ID: 473828)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{1}{3}[/math], sin 3 [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{27}{31}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{-23}{27}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{23}{27}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{9}{11}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}\sin \theta & =\frac{1}{3} \\\therefore \sin 3 \theta & =3 \sin \theta-4 \sin ^{3} \theta \\& =3 \cdot \frac{1}{3}-4 \cdot\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{3} \\& =1-4 \cdot \frac{1}{27} \\& =\frac{27-4}{27}=\frac{23}{27}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

B. [math]\tan 15^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]\cos 75^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 75^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}& \frac{1+\tan 30^{\circ}}{1-\tan 30^{\circ}} \\= & \frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 30^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \tan 30^{\circ}} \quad\left[\because \tan (A+B)=\frac{\tan \mathrm{A}+\tan \mathrm{B}}{1-\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{~B}}\right] \\= & \tan \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \\= & \tan 75^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]

Question:
[math]\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(150^{\circ}+A\right)[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{1}{2} \cos A[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]\cos A[/math]
D. [math]\sin A[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}& \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(150^{\circ}+A\right) \\= & \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(180^{\circ}-30^{\circ}+A\right) \\= & \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left\{180^{\circ}-\left(30^{\circ}-A\right)\right\} \\= & \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(30^{\circ}-A\right) \\= & \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left\{-\left(A-30^{\circ}\right)\right\} \\= & \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)-\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right) \\= & 0\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #126 (ID: 473831)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a=2, b=1, \angle C=60^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
এখানে, [math]a=2, b=1[/math]
 এবং [math]\angle C=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times a b \sin C[/math]
 [math]‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌=\frac{1}{2} \times 2 \times 1 \times \sin 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌‌=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ একক

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\operatorname{cosec}\left(-330^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]-2[/math]
B. [math]\frac{-2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
D. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\operatorname{cosec}[/math]
 [math]\left(-330^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\operatorname{cosec} 330^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -\operatorname{cosec}[/math]
 [math]\left(4 \times 90^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\left(-\operatorname{cosec} 30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]

Question:
[math]n[/math] একটি পূর্ণসংখ্যা হলে, [math]\sin \left\{2 n \pi+(-1)^{2 n} \frac{\pi}{6}\right\}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \left\{2 n \pi+(-1)^{2 n} \frac{\pi}{6}\right\}=\sin \left\{2 n \pi+\frac{\pi}{6}\right\}=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{1}{2}[/math]

Question #129 (ID: 473834)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin ^{4}\theta-\cos^{4}\theta[/math] সমান-

Options:
A. [math]1+2 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
B. [math]1+2 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
C. [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
D. [math]2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin^{4}\theta-\cos^{4}\theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\sin^{2}\theta+\cos^{2}\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(\sin^{2}\theta-\cos^{2}\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\sin^{2}\theta-\cos^{2}\theta[/math]
 [math]=\sin^{2}\theta-\left(1-\sin^{2}\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=2\sin^{2}\theta-1[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]\mathrm {AC}[/math] বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য --

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{25+12\sqrt{2}}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{25-12\sqrt{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{13}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{37}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sqrt{25-12\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm { \cos 45^{\circ}=\dfrac{4^{2}+3^{2}-A C^{2}}{2 \times 4 \times 3} }\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\dfrac{16+9-A C^{2}}{24} \Rightarrow \dfrac{24}{\sqrt{2}}=25-A^{2} }\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { A C^{2}=25-12 \sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm {AC = \sqrt{25-12\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [ [math]\because[/math]
 দৈর্ঘ্য সর্বদা ধনাত্মক]

Question #133 (ID: 473822)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm {ABC}[/math] এ [math]\mathrm {AB = 12}[/math] সে.মি., [math]\mathrm {BC = 5}[/math] সে.মি., [math]\mathrm {AC = 13}[/math] সে.মি. হলে-

[math]\text {i.} ~~~\quad \mathrm {\angle B = \dfrac{\pi}{2}}[/math] [math]\text {ii.} ~\quad[/math] ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]30[/math] বর্গ সে.মি.

[math]\text {iii.} \quad[/math] ত্রিভুজটির পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস [math]13[/math] সে.মি.

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

[Image]
[math]\textbf {i.}~~~[/math]
 এখানে, [math]\mathrm{AB}^{2}+\mathrm{BC}^{2}=12^{2}+5^{2}=13^{2}=\mathrm{AC}^{2} \therefore \angle \mathrm{B}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\textbf {ii.}~~[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\dfrac{1}{2} \mathrm {× AB × BC}[/math]
 [math]\qquad = \dfrac{1}{2} \times 12 \times 5[/math]
 [math]\qquad =30[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি:[math]\textbf{iii.}~[/math]
 সমকোণী ত্রিভুজের পরিব্যাস [math]=[/math]
 সমকোণী ত্রিভুজের অতিভুজ[math]\quad \therefore[/math]
 পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস [math]\mathrm {= AC = 13}[/math]
 সে.মি.সুতরাং, সবগুলো তথ্যই সঠিক

Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


চিত্রের আলোকে কোন সম্পর্কটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math]\sin \mathrm A = 2\sin \mathrm C[/math]
খ. [math]2\sin \mathrm A = \sin \mathrm C[/math]
গ. [math]3\sin \mathrm A = 2\sin \mathrm C[/math]
ঘ. [math]2\sin \mathrm A = 3\sin \mathrm C[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm A = 2\sin \mathrm C[/math]

Explanation:
চিত্রে, [math]\mathrm {BC = a = 6}[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm {AB = c = 3}[/math]
 [math]\text {Sine}[/math]
 সূত্র অনুসারে,[math]\mathrm {\dfrac{a}{\sin A}=\dfrac{c}{\sin C} \Rightarrow \dfrac{6}{\sin A}=\dfrac{3}{\sin C} \therefore \sin A=2 \sin C}[/math]

Question:

Options:
ক. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{7}{8}\right)[/math]
খ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{5}{48}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(-\dfrac{1}{4}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{1}{4}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{-1}\left(-\dfrac{1}{4}\right)[/math]

Explanation:
স্থূলকোণটির পরিমাণ [math]=\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{4^{2}+6^{2}-8^{2}}{2.4 .6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{16+36-64}{48}\right)=\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{-12}{48}\right)=\cos ^{-1}\left(-\dfrac{1}{4}\right)[/math]

Question #137 (ID: 473821)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm {ABC}[/math] এ [math]\mathrm {\angle B=60^{\circ}, \angle C=30^{\circ}}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm b = 3\sqrt{3}[/math] একক হলে [math]\mathrm c[/math] এর দৈর্ঘ্য কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math] একক
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math] একক
C. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math] একক
D. 3 একক


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
3 একক

Explanation:
[math]\triangle \mathrm {ABC}[/math]
 হতে [math]\text {sine}[/math]
 সূত্র অনুসারে, [math]\mathrm {\dfrac{b}{\sin B}=\dfrac{c}{\sin C}}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\Rightarrow c=b \times \dfrac{\sin C}{\sin B}=3 \sqrt{3} \times \dfrac{\sin 30^{\circ}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}=3 \sqrt{3} \times \dfrac{\dfrac{1}{2}}{\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}=3}[/math]
 একক।

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. }~ \quad \sin \theta=\dfrac{3}{5}\\ \text{ii. } \quad \cos ^{2} \theta=\dfrac{16}{25} \\ \text{iii.} \quad\operatorname{cosec} \theta \cdot \sec \theta=\dfrac{25}{12}\end{array}[/math]

 নং তথ্যটি সঠিক নয়। কারণ, ৩য় চতুর্ভাগে [math]\sin \theta[/math]

Question #142 (ID: 473808)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023, 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{-1-\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{2-\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{1+\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{2+\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ} \\=\left(\sin 75^{\circ}\right)^{2} \\=\left[\sin \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)\right]^{2} \\=\left[\sin 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}+\cos 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}\right]^{2} \\=\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)\right)^{2} \\=\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}\right)^{2} \\=\frac{3+1+2 \sqrt{3}}{4(2)} \\=\frac{4+2 \sqrt{3}}{8} \\=\frac{2+\sqrt{3}}{4}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}2 \sin ^{2} 75^{\circ}=1-\cos \left(2 \times 75^{\circ}\right) \\=1-\cos 150^{\circ}=1-\cos \left(180^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right) \\=1+\cos 30^{\circ}=1+\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\dfrac{2+\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Question #143 (ID: 473809)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm {A+B=\dfrac{\pi}{4}}[/math] হলে, [math]\mathrm {\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} \mathbf{B}}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}~ \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
B. [math]\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} ~\sin(\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A})[/math]
C. [math]\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2} ~\cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
D. [math]\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2} ~\sin (\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A})[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}[/math]
 [math]=-\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B) \\=-\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \sin (A-B) \\=-\sin (A-B)=\sin (B-A)\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B=\sin (B+A) \sin (B-A) } \\\mathrm {=\sin \dfrac{\pi}{4} \cdot \sin (B-A)=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin (B-A)}\end{array}[/math]

Question:
[math]\mathrm {A+B=\dfrac{\pi}{2}}[/math] হলে নিম্নের কোনটি সঠিক ?

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm {\tan A=\tan B}[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm {\tan A=-\tan B}[/math]
গ. [math]\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}=-1[/math]
ঘ. [math]\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}=1[/math]

Explanation:
যদি [math]\mathrm {A+B=\dfrac{\pi}{2}}[/math]
 হয় তবে,[math]\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}=\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{A}\right)=\tan \mathrm{A} \cdot \cot \mathrm{A}=1[/math]

Question #146 (ID: 473812)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023, 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board, Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm {\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(150^{\circ}+A\right)}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. 0
B. [math]\dfrac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\mathrm {2 \sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)}[/math]
D. [math]\sin \mathrm A[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:


Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left(150^{\circ}+A\right) } \\ =\mathrm{\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)+\sin \left\{180^{\circ}+\left(A-30^{\circ}\right)\right\}} \\ = \mathrm{\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)-\sin \left(A-30^{\circ}\right)=0}\end{array}[/math]

Question:
[math]\sqrt{4 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{24}}[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2-\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2-\sqrt{3}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math]

Explanation:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sqrt{4 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{24}}=\sqrt{2\left(1-\cos \dfrac{\pi}{12}\right)}=\sqrt{2-2 \cos \dfrac{\pi}{12}} \\=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{12}}}=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \dfrac{\pi}{6}\right)}} \\=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2 \cdot \dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}}=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}\end{array}[/math]
