Question #150 (ID: 473816)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলির দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]\text {6 cm, 8 cm }[/math] এবং [math]\text {10 cm}[/math] । ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ কত?

Options:
ক. 6 cm
খ. 7 cm
গ. 8 cm
ঘ. 5 cm


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
5 cm

Explanation:
[math]8^{2}+6^{2}=64+36=100=10^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী ত্রিভুজ যার অতিভুজ [math]\text {10 cm.}[/math]
আমরা জানি, সমকোণী ত্রিভুজের পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]= \dfrac{1}{2} \times[/math]
 অতিভুজের দৈর্ঘ্য [math]= \dfrac{1}{2} × 10 = \text {5 cm}[/math]

Question:
[math]\tan \dfrac{\theta}{2}=\dfrac{3}{4}[/math] হলে [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{9}{16}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{24}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{25}{7}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Explanation:
[math]\cos \theta=\dfrac{1-\tan ^{2} \dfrac{\theta}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \dfrac{\theta}{2}}=\dfrac{1-\left(\dfrac{3}{4}\right)^{2}}{1+\left(\dfrac{3}{4}\right)^{2}}=\dfrac{7}{25}[/math]

Question #152 (ID: 473734)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Comilla Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের চিত্রের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]\frac{a}{c}=?[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
এখানে, [math]A=180^{\circ}-120^{\circ}-30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{c}{\sin C} \quad[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{a}{c}=\frac{\sin A}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 30^{\circ}}{\sin 120^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{1}{2}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Explanation:

খ. [math]2[/math]

ঘ. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

 [math]\therefore \frac{2}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4=2 \mathrm{R} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{R}=2[/math]

Question:

Options:
A. [math]17.93 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
B. [math]37.55 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
C. [math]40.20 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
D. [math]50.98 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\text { sin }[/math]
 সূত্রানুসারে, [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b^{}}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{b}=\frac{\sin \mathrm{B}}{\sin \mathrm{A}} \cdot \mathrm{a}=\frac{\sin 27^{\circ}}{\sin 81^{\circ}} \times 39=17.93 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

Question #163 (ID: 473723)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka City College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলোর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]13, 14[/math] ও [math]15[/math] একক হলে, অন্তঃব্যাসার্ধ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]8[/math] একক
খ. [math]6[/math] একক
গ. [math]4[/math] একক
ঘ. [math]2[/math] একক


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
অর্ধপরিসীমা, [math]s=\frac{13+14+15}{2}[/math]
 [math]=21[/math]
অন্তঃব্যাসার্ধ, [math]r=\frac{\Delta}{s}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}}{s}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{21(21-13)(21-15)(21-14)}}{21}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{84}{21}=4[/math]
 একক

Explanation:

Question #166 (ID: 473726)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: SCOT
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর [math]b=2, c=\sqrt{2}[/math] এবং [math]\angle B=45^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]a[/math] বাহুর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]1+\sqrt{3}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}-1[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
আমরা জানি, [math]\cos B=\frac{c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}}{2 c a}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\cos 45^{\circ}=\frac{(\sqrt{2})^{2}+a^{2}-(2)^{2}}{2 \times \sqrt{2} a}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\frac{2+a^{2}-4}{2 \sqrt{2} a} \text{ Or, } a^{2}-2 a-2=0\\\Rightarrow a^{2}-2 a+1=3 \Rightarrow (a-1)^{2}=3\\\Rightarrow a-1=\sqrt{3} \Rightarrow a=\sqrt{3}+1\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #170 (ID: 473701)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: সফিউদ্দিন সরকার একাডেমি এন্ড কলেজ
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 18^{\circ}+\cos 18^{\circ}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sin 36^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2} \cos 27^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]-\sqrt{2 \cos 27^{\circ}}[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin 18^{\circ}+\cos 18^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \sin 18^{\circ}+\sin \left(90^{\circ}-18^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin 18^{\circ}+\sin 72^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \left(\frac{18^{\circ}+72^{\circ}}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{72^{\circ}-18^{\circ}}{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin 45^{\circ} \cos 27^{\circ}=\sqrt{2} \cos 27^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #171 (ID: 473704)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Girl's Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A}+\mathbf{B}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\cos ^{2} B-\sin ^{2} A[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]\cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
C. [math]\sin (B-A)[/math]
D. [math]-\cos (\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A})[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
আমরা জানি ,[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{~A} =\cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]=0 \cdot \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #172 (ID: 473705)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Rajuk Uttara Model College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin x+\sin y=1[/math] এবং [math]\cos x+\cos y=0[/math] হলে [math](x+y)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\pi[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin x+\sin y=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=1 \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\cos x+\cos y=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=0......(ii)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(ii) } \div \text{ (i) } \Rightarrow \cot \frac{x+y}{2}=0=\cot \frac{\pi}{2}\\\Rightarrow \frac{x+y}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore x+y=\pi\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #173 (ID: 473706)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Govt Azizul Haque College, Bogura
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2 \sin \frac{\pi}{16}[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]2 \sin \frac{\pi}{2^{n}}=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{\ldots+\sqrt{(n-1)}}}}}}[/math]
 তম 2[math]\therefore 2 \sin \frac{\pi}{16}=2 \sin \frac{\pi}{2^{4}}=\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #175 (ID: 473708)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: CITY COLLEGE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1+\sin x}{\cos x}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
B. [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
C. [math]\cot \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1+\sin x}{\cos x}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+2 \sin \frac{x}{2} \cos \frac{x}{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)^{2}}{\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{x}{2}}\left[\cos \frac{x}{2}\right.[/math]
 দ্বারা লব ও হরকে ভাগ করে ][math]\Rightarrow\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #182 (ID: 473716)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022, 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Barisal Cadet College, Monipur High School and College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হয়, তাহলে [math]\angle {A}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\pi[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos A+\cos C=\sin B \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{B}{2}\right) \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=\sin B \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}=\mathrm{B}\\\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{~A}=\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi \quad \therefore \mathrm{A}=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #183 (ID: 473718)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Rajuk Uttara Model College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হলে, [math]A=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\text { Or,} b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}=bc[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a : b : c = 3 : 7 : 5[/math] হলে, [math]B[/math] এর মান —

Options:
ক. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos B=\frac{3^{2}+5^{2}-7^{2}}{2.3 .5}=\frac{-1}{2}=\cos 120^{\circ} \\\therefore B=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Question #186 (ID: 473684)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Barisal Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math] হলে [math]\cos \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4}{5}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{3}{4}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{4}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta=\frac{9}{25}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-\cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{9}{25}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=1-\frac{9}{25}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{25-9}{25}=\frac{16}{25}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=\pm \frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta=-\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi\right.[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\cos \theta[/math]
 ঋণাত্মক ]

Explanation:

Question #190 (ID: 473689)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Holy Cross College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{12}{13}, 270^{\circ}<\theta<360^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\sin \theta+\sec \theta}{\cos \theta-\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{109}{209}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{209}{160}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{-160}{209}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{-209}{160}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos \theta=\frac{12}{13} \\\therefore \sin \theta=\sqrt{1-\left(\frac{12}{13}\right)^{2}}=-\frac{5}{13} \quad\left[\because 270^{\circ}<\theta<360^{\circ}\right] \\\therefore \tan \theta=\frac{-\frac{5}{13}}{\frac{12}{13}}=-\frac{5}{12}, \sec \theta=\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{13}{12} \\\therefore \frac{\sin \theta+\sec \theta}{\cos \theta-\tan \theta}=\frac{-\frac{5}{13}+\frac{13}{12}}{\frac{12}{13}+\frac{5}{12}}=\frac{109}{209} \\\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #193 (ID: 473692)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Ahammad Uddin Shah Shishu Niketon School & College, Gaibandha
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 45^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{4}{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 45^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \left\{\sin \left(90^{\circ}-75^{\circ}\right)\right\}^{2}+\left(\sin 45^{\circ}\right)^{2}+\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow\cos ^{2} 75^{\circ}+\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}+\sin ^{2} 75^{\circ}=1+\frac{1}{2}=\frac{3}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #194 (ID: 473693)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Holy Cross College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4} ; 180^{\circ}<\theta<270^{\circ}[/math] হলে,

i. [math]\cot \theta=\frac{4}{3}[/math]

ii. [math]\cos \theta<0[/math]

iii. [math]\tan 3 \theta=-\frac{117}{44}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. ii
B. i ও ii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
i, ii ও iii

Explanation:

Question #195 (ID: 473694)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Ideal School & College, Motijheel, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{2})[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt{3}-1)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt{3}+1)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}, \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{2 \sqrt{2}}(\sqrt{3}-1)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})[/math]


Explanation:

Question #197 (ID: 473696)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka Imperial College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}=\frac{2 \cos \frac{75^{\circ}+15^{\circ}}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{75^{\circ}-15^{\circ}}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{75^{\circ}+15^{\circ}}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{75^{\circ}-15^{\circ}}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ}}{\sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}}=\cot 45^{\circ} \cdot \tan 30^{\circ}=1, \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \\\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #198 (ID: 473697)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahid Syed Nazrul Islam College, Mymensingh
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan A \tan B=1[/math] হলে [math]\mathbf{A}+\mathbf{B}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. মান নেই


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\tan (A+B)=\frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \tan B}=\frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-1}=\infty \\\therefore A+B=\tan ^{-1}(\infty)=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]2 \sin \left(60^{\circ}-x\right) \sin \left(60^{\circ}+x\right)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2}+\sin 2 x[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}-\sin 2 x[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}+\cos 2 x[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}-\cos 2 x[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}2 \sin \left(60^{\circ}-x\right) \sin \left(60^{\circ}+x\right) \\\Rightarrow \cos \left(60^{\circ}-x-60^{\circ}-x\right)-\cos \left(60^{\circ}-x+60^{\circ}+x\right) \\\Rightarrow\cos (-2 x)-\cos \left(120^{\circ}\right)=\cos 2 x+\frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]a=6, b=3 \sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]A=90^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B} \\\Rightarrow \frac{6}{\sin 90^{\circ}}=\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{\sin B} \\\Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin \frac{\pi}{3} \\\therefore B=\frac{\pi}{3}\end{array}[/math]

Question #203 (ID: 473678)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{3}{5}[/math] এবং [math]\cos B=\frac{12}{13}[/math] হলে-

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. } \sin (A-B)=\frac{16}{65}\\\text{ii. } \cos (A+B)=\frac{63}{65}\\\text{iii. } \tan A+\tan B=\frac{7}{6}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. ii ও iii
C. i ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\text { (i) } \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=\sin A \cos B-\cos A \sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin A \cos B-\sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} A} \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{3}{5} \frac{12}{13}-\sqrt{1-\left(\frac{3}{5}\right)^{2}} \sqrt{1-\left(\frac{12}{13}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{36}{65}-\frac{4}{5} \cdot \frac{5}{13}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{36}{65}-\frac{4}{13}=\frac{16}{65}[/math]
 [math]\text{(ii) } \cos (A+B)=\cos A \cos B-\sin A \sin B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4}{5} \frac{12}{13}-\frac{3}{5} \frac{5}{13}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{48-15}{65}=\frac{33}{65}[/math]
 [math]\text{(iii) } \tan A+\tan B=\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}+\frac{\sin B}{\cos B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{3}{5}}{\frac{4}{5}}+\frac{\frac{5}{13}}{\frac{12}{13}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{4}+\frac{5}{12}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{14}{12}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{7}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sec \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=0[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}=\frac{1}{\sin \theta} \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=1 \quad \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4} \end{array}[/math]

Question #211 (ID: 473666)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\sec \boldsymbol{A}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{5}{7}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{7}{9}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{28}{45}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\\frac{35}{29}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos A^{\circ}=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c} \Rightarrow \sec A=\frac{2 b c}{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \sec A=\frac{2 \times 5 \times 7}{5^{2}+7^{2}-4^{2}} \therefore \sec A=\frac{35}{29}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
D. [math]-\tan ^{2} \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

 [math]=-\sin \theta \sec \theta \cdot \cot \left(7 \times 90^{\circ}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -\sin \theta \sec \theta(-\tan \theta)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\tan ^{2} \theta[/math]

Question #215 (ID: 473664)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


উদ্দীপকের ক্ষেত্রে—

i. [math]A=43.85^{\circ}[/math]

ii. ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]\frac{20}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]

iii. [math]\sec B=2[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text{i. } \Delta=\frac{1}{2} b c \sin A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin A=\frac{2 \Delta}{b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \times 7 \sqrt{3}}{5 \times 7}=\frac{2 \sqrt{3}}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}=43.85^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\text{ii. } \frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin B}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{5}{2 \sin 60^{\circ}}=R[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow R=\frac{5}{2 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\text { iii. } \sec B=\frac{1}{\cos B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos 60^{\circ}}=2[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #216 (ID: 473660)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

 [math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sin 45^{\circ}}=\frac{A B}{\sin 60^{\circ}} \\\therefore A B=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}} \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]

Question #217 (ID: 473662)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\cos 8^{\circ}+\sin 8^{\circ}}{\cos 8^{\circ}-\sin 8^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\tan 37^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]\tan 53^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]\tan 52^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 68^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cos 8^{\circ}\left(1+\tan 8^{\circ}\right)}{\cos 8^{\circ}\left(1-1 \cdot \tan 8^{\circ}\right)}=\frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 8^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \cdot \tan 8^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \tan \left(45^{\circ}+8^{\circ}\right)=\tan 53^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #218 (ID: 473663)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল -

i. [math]10 \sin \mathrm{C}[/math]

ii. [math]7 \sqrt{3}[/math]

iii. [math]16 \mathrm{r}, \mathrm{r}[/math] ত্রিভুজটির অন্তঃব্যাসার্ধ

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 4 \times 5 \times \sin C=10 \sin C[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 4 \times 7 \times \sin 60^{\circ}=14 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=7 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2}(a+b+c) r=8 r[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

[Image]


পাশের [math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে—

i. [math]\frac{a}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin C}[/math]

ii. ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} b c \cos A[/math]

iii. [math]\cos B=\frac{c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}}{2 c a}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. ii ও iii
C. i ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
(ii) সঠিক নয়' কারণ ত্রিভুয়োর ফেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} a b \sin A[/math]

Question #222 (ID: 473656)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলির পরিমাপ [math]3 \mathrm{~cm}, 5 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] ও [math]7 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] হলে-

i. ত্রিভুজটি স্থূলকোণী

ii. স্থূল কোণটির মান [math]120^{\circ}[/math]

iii. [math]3 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] এর বিপরীত কোণটি সূক্ষ্মকোণ

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক ?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
বড় বাহু বিপরীত কোন বড় হয়। এক্ষেত্রে বড় বাহ্ন [math]7cm[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta=\frac{3^{2}+5^{2}-7^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\cos ^{-1}\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ} \quad(i+i i)[/math]
 সঠিক।(iii) ছোট বাহুর বিপরীত কোম সূক্ষ্ম কোণ হয়। এক্ষেত্রে [math]3 cm[/math]
 বাহুটি সবথেকে ছোটো।

Explanation:

Question #223 (ID: 473651)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{4}{5}[/math] হলে [math]\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{7}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{7}{5}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{7}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin A=\frac{4}{5}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\tan A=\frac{4}{3}[/math]
 [math]\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\frac{16}{9}}{1+\frac{16}{9}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\frac{-7}{9}}{\frac{25}{9}} \\=-\frac{7}{25}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #224 (ID: 473652)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cos B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos (A+B)[/math] এর মান কত হবে ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{6}+1}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2} \sqrt{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2 \sqrt{6}-1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{6}+1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin A=\frac{1}{2} \\\therefore A=30^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\cos B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \\\therefore B=45^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\cos (A+B)=\cos A[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos B-\sin A \cdot \sin B[/math]
 [math]=\cos 30^{\circ} \cos 45^{\circ}-\sin 30^{\circ} \cdot \sin 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}-\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \\=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #225 (ID: 473653)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1-\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}{1+\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\cot \theta[/math]
B. [math]\tan \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sin \theta+\cos \theta[/math]
D. [math]\sin \theta-\cos \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1-\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}{1+\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta}{2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{x \sin \theta(\sin \theta+\cos \theta)}{2 \cos \theta(\sin \theta+\cos \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \theta[/math]


Explanation:

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii

ঘ. i, ii ও iii

Question #229 (ID: 473636)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(\sin 50^{\circ}+\sin 70^{\circ}-\cos 80^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
E. No correct answer


Correct Answer: .

Solution:
[math]\sin 50^{\circ}+\sin 70^{\circ} -\cos 80^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\cos \left(90^{\circ}-10^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos 10^{\circ}-\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \cos 10^{\circ}-\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #233 (ID: 473640)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1+\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}{1-\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\cos \theta[/math]
B. [math]\sin \theta[/math]
C. [math]\cot \theta[/math]
D. [math]-\cot \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1+\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}{1-\cos 2 \theta+\sin 2 \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}{2 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{2 \cos \theta(\cos \theta+\sin \theta)}{2 \sin \theta(\cos \theta+\sin \theta)}=\cot \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #238 (ID: 473645)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] হলে, [math]\cos 2 \theta=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]
C. [math]2\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 \theta=2 \cos \theta-1[/math]
 [math]=2 \cdot\left[\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)\right]^{2}-1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)+1 \\=\frac{1}{2} x^{2}+1+\frac{1}{2 x^{2}}-1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #239 (ID: 473646)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{3}{5}[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{1+\tan A}{1-\tan A}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]-7[/math]
B. [math]7[/math]
C. [math]\frac{4}{7}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{1}{7}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin A=\frac{3}{5} \\\tan A=\frac{3}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1+\tan A}{1-\tan A} =\frac{1+\frac{3}{4}}{1-\frac{3}{4}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{7}{4}}{\frac{1}{4}} .[/math]
 [math]=7[/math]


Explanation:

Question #241 (ID: 473648)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \left(45^{\circ}+\theta\right) \cos \left(45^{\circ}-\theta\right)-\sin \left(45^{\circ}+\theta\right) \sin \left(45^{\circ}-\theta\right)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos \left(45^{\circ}+\theta\right) \cdot \cos[/math]
 [math]\left(45^{\circ}-\theta\right)-\sin \left(45^{\circ}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sin \left(45^{\circ}-\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(45^{\circ}+\theta+45^{\circ}-\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #242 (ID: 473649)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin ^{2} 0+\sin ^{2}[/math] [math]10^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 20^{\circ}+[/math] [math]\ldots \ldots+\sin ^{2} 90^{\circ}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]10[/math]
B. [math]16[/math]
C. [math]5[/math]
D. [math]20[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} 0+\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\ldots+\sin ^{2} 80^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=0+\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}+\cdots \sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left(90^{\circ}-10^{\circ}\right)+1[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\ldots+\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 10^{\circ}+1[/math]
 [math]=1+1+1+1+1=5[/math]


Explanation:

Question #243 (ID: 473650)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos 2 A+\cos \left(2 A+120^{\circ}\right)+\cos \left(120^{\circ}-2 A\right)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\cos 2 A[/math]
B. [math]-\cos 2 A[/math]
C. [math]0[/math]
D. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 A[/math]
 [math]+\cos \left(2 A+120^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos \left(120^{\circ}-2 A\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 A+[/math]
 [math]\cos \left\{90^{\circ}+\left(30^{\circ}+2 A\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\cos \left\{90^{\circ}+\left(30^{\circ}-2 A\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 A[/math]
 [math]-\sin \left(30^{\circ}+2 A\right)-\sin[/math]
 [math]\left(30^{\circ} - 2 A\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 A-[/math]
 [math]\left\{\sin \left(30^{\circ}+2 A\right)+\sin \left(30^{\circ}-2 A\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 A-\left\{2 \sin 30^{\circ} \cdot \cos 2 A\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 A-2 \cdot \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos 2 A[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #244 (ID: 473630)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]b=3[/math] একক হলে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল কত বর্গ একক?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{9}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{C}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\therefore c=\frac{1}{2} \times 2 \times 1[/math]
 [math]\therefore c=1[/math]
 একক ; [math]\text { Given, } b=3[/math]
 এককক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times b \times c \times \sin A[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2} \times 3 \times 1 \times \sin ^{\circ}\left(30^{\circ}\right) \\=\frac{1}{2} \times 3 \times \frac{1}{2} \\=\frac{3}{4}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #247 (ID: 473629)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\frac{c+a}{b}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]2[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\angle C=180^{\circ}-\left(120^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\frac{a}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=\frac{b}{\sin 120^{\circ}}=\frac{c}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \frac{a}{\frac{1}{2}} & =2 \times 1 \\\therefore a & =1\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{c}{\frac{1}{2}}=2 \times 1 \\\therefore c=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{b}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}=2 \\\therefore b=r_{3}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]f(x)=\cos x[/math] হলে, [math]f^{\prime \prime}\left(\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math] এর সমান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}f(x)=\cos x \\f^{\prime}(x)=-\sin x \\\therefore f^{\prime \prime}(x)=-\cos x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore f^{\prime \prime}(\pi / 3)[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \pi / 3=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]

Question #254 (ID: 473622)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]\frac{\cot B-1}{\cot B+1}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\cot B-1}{\cot B+1}=\frac{\cot 15^{\circ}-1}{\cot 15^{\circ}+1}[/math]
 [চিত্র হতে পাই, [math]\left.B=15^{\circ}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cot 45^{\circ} \cot 15^{\circ}-1}{\cot 15^{\circ}+\cot 45^{\circ}} \quad\left[\because \cot 45^{\circ}=1\right] \\\Rightarrow \cot \left(45^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)=\cot 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #257 (ID: 473587)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]D[/math] বিন্দুর স্থানাঙ্ক কত?

Options:
ক. [math](0.93,0)[/math]
খ. [math](0.48,0)[/math]
গ. [math](0.52,0)[/math]
ঘ. [math](0.71,0)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\mathrm{AB}}{\sin 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sin 135^{\circ}} \therefore A B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2}}{2}[/math]
এখন, [math]\angle \mathrm{BAD}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{x}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{135^{\circ}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{BAD}[/math]
 এ [math]\frac{\mathrm{AB}}{\sin \left(180^{\circ}-30^{\circ}-\frac{135^{\circ}}{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{BD}}{\sin \frac{135^{\circ}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{BD}=0.48[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{D}[/math]
 বিন্দুর স্থানাঙ্ক [math](0.48,0)[/math]

Question:
যদি, [math]\tan =\frac{3}{4}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\sec 2 A[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]-\frac{25}{7}[/math]
খ. [math]-\frac{7}{5}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{7}{5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{25}{7}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l} \sec 2 A=\frac{1}{\cos 2 A}=\frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}=\frac{1+\left(\frac{3}{4}\right)^{2}}{1-\left(\frac{3}{4}\right)^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{16+9}{16-9}=\frac{25}{7}\end{array}[/math]

Question:
যদি একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহুসমূহ যথাক্রমে [math]m, n[/math] এবং [math]\sqrt{m^{2}+m n+n^{2}}[/math] একক হয় তবে ত্রিভুজটির বৃহত্তম কোণ এর মান কত

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
বৃহত্তম কোণ A হলে,[math]\cos A=\frac{m^{2}+n^{2}-m^{2}-m n-n^{2}}{2 m n}=-\frac{1}{2} \therefore A=120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math][\because[/math]
 বৃহত্তম বাহু [math]\left.\sqrt{m^{2}+m n+n^{2}}\right][/math]

Question #261 (ID: 473591)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যেকোনো ' [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]\tan \frac{A}{2} \cdot \tan \frac{B}{2}+\tan \frac{B}{2} \cdot \tan \frac{C}{2}+\tan \frac{C}{2} \cdot \tan \frac{A}{2}[/math] = কত?

Options:
A. [math]\tan \left( A+B+c\right)[/math]
B. [math]\tan \left( \dfrac{A+B+C}{2}\right)[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan \left(\frac{A}{2}+\frac{B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cot \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan \frac{A}{2}+\tan \frac{B}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{A}{2} \cdot \tan \frac{B}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\tan \frac{C}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \frac{A}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \tan \frac{B}{2}+\tan \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \tan \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]+\tan \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \tan \frac{A}{2}=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #265 (ID: 473595)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sum_{n=0}^{100} \cot (n \pi+\theta)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]101 \cot \theta[/math]
B. [math]100 \cot \theta[/math]
C. [math]100 \tan \theta[/math]
D. [math]101 \tan \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sum_{n=0}^{100} \cot (n \pi+\theta)[/math]
 [math]\therefore n=0[/math]
 হলে, [math]\cot (0+\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\cot \theta[/math]
লক্ষ্য করি, [math]\cot (\pi+\theta)=[/math]
 [math]\cot (2 \pi+\theta)=[/math]
 [math]\cot (3 \pi+\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\ldots \ldots=\cot \theta[/math]
এভাবে, [math]n = 1[/math]
 থেকে [math]n = 100[/math]
 পর্যন্ত মোট [math]100[/math]
টি [math]\cot \theta[/math]
 পাওয়া যায়।[math]\therefore \sum_{n=0}^{100} \cot (n \pi+\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\cot \theta+100 \cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=101 \cot \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #266 (ID: 473596)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec x+\tan x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+x\right)[/math]
B. [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
C. [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+x\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sec x+\tan x[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos x}+\frac{\sin x}{\cos x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{1+\sin x}{\cos x}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+2 \sin \frac{x}{2} \cos \frac{x}{2}}{\cos 2 \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{\left(\sin \frac{x}{2}+\cos \frac{x}{2}\right)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{1+\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [লব ও হরকে [math]\cos \frac{x}{2}[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\Rightarrow\frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}+\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \cdot \tan \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #268 (ID: 473598)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]1+\tan 2 A \tan A=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sec A[/math]
B. [math]\cos 2 A[/math]
C. [math]\sec 2 A[/math]
D. [math]\operatorname{cosec} 2 A[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]1+\tan 2 A \tan A=1+\frac{2 \tan A}{1-\tan ^{2} A} \cdot \tan A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\frac{2 \tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A+2 \tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\left(\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos 2 A}[/math]
 [math]=\sec 2 A[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

Options:
A. [math]4[/math]
B. [math]5[/math]
C. [math]3[/math]
D. [math]4.5[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} 0+\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\ldots+\sin ^{2} 80^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=0+\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}+\cdots \sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left(90^{\circ}-10^{\circ}\right)+1[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 10^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\ldots+\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 10^{\circ}+1[/math]
 [math]=1+1+1+1+1=5[/math]

Question #270 (ID: 473600)

Question:
[math]C+D=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math] হলে, [math](1+\tan C)(1+\tan D)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]4[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan (C+D)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{4}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan C+\tan D}{1-\tan C \cdot \tan D}[/math]
 [math]=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan C+\tan[/math]
 [math]D+\tan C \tan D=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\tan C+\tan D[/math]
 [math](1+\tan C)=1+1=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (1+\tan C)[/math]
 [math](1+\tan D)=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]2 \cos \frac{\pi}{16}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}2 \cos \frac{\pi}{16}=\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}}=\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{8}\right)} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{2+2 \cos \frac{\pi}{8}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}\end{array}[/math]

Question #273 (ID: 473603)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের দুটি বাহু [math]4[/math] একক ও [math]3[/math] একক এবং ক্ষেত্রফল [math]3[/math] বর্গ একক হলে অন্তর্ভুক্ত কোণের পরিমাণ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]15^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
মনে করি, ত্রিভুজের বাহু দুটি [math]a[/math]
 ও [math]b[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\Delta[/math]
 এবং অন্তর্ভুক্ত কোণ [math]C[/math]
.[math]\therefore \Delta=\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{ab} \sin \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3=\frac{1}{2} \times 4[/math]
 [math]\times 3 \times \sin \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \mathrm{C}=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin C=\sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=30^{\circ} \text {. }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #274 (ID: 473604)

Question:
[math]n[/math] যেকোনো ধনাত্মক বিজোড় সংখ্যা হলে [math]\sin \left\{n \pi+(-1)^{n} \frac{\pi}{3}\right\}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{-\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]n[/math]
 বিজোড় সংখ্যা হলে, [math]n=2 m+1 ; m \in \mathbb{Z}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \left\{(2 m+1) \pi+(-1)^{2 m+1} \frac{\pi}{3}\right\} \\\Rightarrow \sin \left\{2 m \pi+\pi+(-1)^{2 m}(-1) \frac{\pi}{3}\right\} \\\Rightarrow \sin \left\{\pi-\frac{\pi}{3}\right\}=\sin \frac{\pi}{3}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

B. [math]\tan 54^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]\tan 42^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 24^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

 [লব ও হরকে [math]\cos 9^{\circ}[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 9^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \tan 9^{\circ}}\left[\because \tan 45^{\circ}=1\right] \\\Rightarrow \tan \left(45^{\circ}+9^{\circ}\right)=\tan 54^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Question #288 (ID: 473619)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

[math]\cot \theta=\frac{12}{5}[/math] এবং [math]\cos \theta[/math] ধনাত্মক

Question #290 (ID: 473584)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\mathrm{b}=9 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] এবং [math]A=115^{\circ}[/math] [math]AD[/math] এর দৈর্ঘ্য কত সে.মি.?

Options:
ক. [math]1.585[/math]
খ. [math]2.87[/math]
গ. [math]3.4[/math]
ঘ. [math]4.32[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l} a=\sqrt{b^{2}+c^{2}-2 b c \cos A} \\\Rightarrow\sqrt{9^{2}+5^{2}-2 \times 9 \times 5 \times \cos \left(115^{\circ}\right)}=12 \\\Delta=\frac{1}{2} \times b c \times \sin A=\frac{1}{2} \times a \times A D \\\therefore A D=\frac{b c \sin A}{a}=\frac{9 \times 5 \times \sin \left(115^{\circ}\right)}{12}=3.4\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #291 (ID: 473585)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\mathrm{b}=9 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] এবং [math]A=115^{\circ}[/math] [math]D[/math] বিন্দু [math]BC[/math] কে কত অনুপাতে অন্তর্বিভক্ত করে (প্রায়)?

Options:
ক. [math]11: 25[/math]
খ. [math]13: 30[/math]
গ. [math]3.4[/math]
ঘ. [math]2: 9[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos B=\frac{a^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}}{2 a c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{12^{2}+5^{2}-9^{2}}{2 \times 12 \times 5}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{11}{15}[/math]
 [math]\cos C=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{12^{2}+9^{2}-5^{2}}{2 \times 12 \times 9}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{25}{27}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{B D}{C D}=\frac{c \cos B}{b \cos C}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5 \times \frac{11}{15}}{9 \times \frac{25}{27}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{11}{25}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{BD}: \mathrm{CD}[/math]
 [math]=11: 25[/math]


Explanation:

Question #293 (ID: 473580)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math] বৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]153.86[/math] বর্গ সে.মি.

[math]\sin 2 C+\sin 2 B-\sin 2 A[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \cos A \cos B \sin C[/math]
খ. [math]4 \sin A \cos B \cos C[/math]
গ. [math]2 \sin A \sin B \cos C[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin 2 C+\sin 2 B-\sin 2 A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin (B+C) \cos (B-C)[/math]
 [math]-2 \sin A \cos A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin (\pi-A) \cos (B-C)[/math]
 [math]-2 \sin A \cos A ;[/math]
 [math][\because A+B+C=\pi][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin A[/math]
 [math][\cos (B-C)[/math]
 [math]-\cos A][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin A[/math]
 [math][\cos (B-C)[/math]
 [math]-\cos \{\pi-(B+C)\}][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin A[/math]
 [math][\cos (B-C)[/math]
 [math]+\cos (B+C)][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4 \sin A[/math]
 [math]\cos B \cos C[/math]


Explanation:

Question #295 (ID: 473573)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল-

i. [math]\Delta=\frac{a b c}{4 R} ; R=[/math] পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ

ii. [math]\Delta=\frac{1}{2} \times(a+b+c) \times r ; r=[/math] অন্তঃবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ

iii. [math]\Delta=\mathrm{s}(\mathrm{s}-\mathrm{a}) \times \cot \left(\frac{\mathrm{A}}{2}\right)[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. ii ও iii
গ. i ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cot \left(\frac{A}{2}\right)=\sqrt{\frac{s(s-a)}{(s-b)(s-c)}} \\\Rightarrow\sqrt{\frac{s^{2}(s-a)^{2}}{s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}}=\frac{s(s-a)}{\Delta} \\\therefore \Delta=s(s-a) / \cot \left(\frac{A}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #298 (ID: 473576)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:

[math]\cot \alpha+\cot \beta=a[/math] এবং [math]\tan \alpha+\tan \beta=b[/math] [math]\tan \alpha . \tan \beta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a}{b}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{b}{a}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a^2}{b^3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{b^2}{a^2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cot \alpha+\cot \beta=a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha}+\frac{\cos \beta}{\sin \beta}=a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \alpha \cdot \sin \beta+\sin \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}=a[/math]
 [math]\frac{\sin (\alpha+\beta)}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}=a....[/math]
(i)এবং [math]\tan \alpha+\tan \beta=b[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}+\frac{\sin \beta}{\cos \beta}=b[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \alpha \cos \beta+\cos \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}=b \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin (\alpha+\beta)}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}=b\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \div \text { (iii) }[/math]
 [math]\frac{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}=b / a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \alpha \cdot \tan \beta=b / a[/math]


Explanation:

Question #299 (ID: 473577)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:

[math]\cot \alpha+\cot \beta=a[/math] এবং [math]\tan \alpha+\tan \beta=b[/math] [math]\tan (\alpha+\beta)=[/math] কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{a b}{a+b}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{a b}{a-b} .[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{a b}{b-a}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{a+b}{a-b}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cot \alpha+\cot \beta=a[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\tan \alpha}+\frac{1}{\tan \beta}=a \\\Rightarrow \frac{\tan \beta+\tan \alpha}{\tan \alpha \cdot \tan \beta}=a \\\Rightarrow \tan \alpha \cdot \tan \beta=\frac{b}{a}\end{array}[/math]
এখন [math]\tan (\alpha+\beta)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\tan \alpha+\tan \beta}{1-\tan \alpha \cdot \tan \beta} \\=\frac{b}{1-b / a}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{b}{\frac{a-b}{a}}=\frac{a b}{a-b}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #300 (ID: 473578)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

[math]\sec 2 x=\frac{1}{a}[/math] [math]\tan x[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1-a}{1+a}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1+a}{1-a}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{\frac{1-a}{1+a}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{\frac{1+a}{1-a}}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec 2 x=\frac{1}{a} \Rightarrow \cos 2 x=a \\\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos 2 x}{1+\cos 2 x}=\frac{1-a}{1+a} \\\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} x=\frac{1-a}{1+a} \\\therefore \tan x=\sqrt{\frac{1-a}{1+a}}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #301 (ID: 473579)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

[math]\sec 2 x=\frac{1}{a}[/math] [math]a=\sin x[/math] হলে, x এর মান কত? [math][0

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sec 2 x=\frac{1}{a}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sin x}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos 2 x[/math]
 [math]=\sin x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin ^{2} x[/math]
 [math]=\sin x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} x+\sin x-1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin ^{2} x+2 \sin x-\sin x-1[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin x(\sin x+1)[/math]
 [math]-1(\sin x+1)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(2 \sin x-1)[/math]
 [math](\sin x+1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin x[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{\pi}{6},[/math]
 [math]\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #304 (ID: 473569)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনো ত্রিভুজে [math]b=2 c[/math] এবং [math]B=3 C[/math] হলে-

i. [math]\sin 3 C=2 \sin C[/math]

ii. [math]\angle \mathrm{C}=30^{\circ}[/math]

iii. ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math][b=2 C, B=3 ][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 c}{\sin 3 c}=\frac{c}{\sin c} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin c=\sin 3 c \\\therefore 2 \sin c=3 \sin c-4 \sin ^{3} \cdot c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{3} C=\sin C \\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} c=\frac{1}{4} \\\Rightarrow \sin c=\frac{1}{2}=\sin 30^{\circ} \\\therefore c=30^{\circ} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore B=3 \times 30^{\circ}=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle A B C[/math]
 সমকোনী

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #305 (ID: 473570)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহু তিনটি যথাক্রমে [math]11, 12, 13[/math] একক হলে

i. ত্রিভুজটি সূক্ষ্মকোণী

ii. ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]61.48[/math] বর্গ একক

iii. ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]7[/math] একক (প্রায়)

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক ?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
(ⅰ) বৃহত্তম কোণ[math]\cos C=\frac{11^{2}+12^{2}-13^{2}}{2 \cdot 11.12}[/math]
 [math]c=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{4}{11}\right)[/math]
 [math]=68.67^{\circ} \rightarrow[/math]
 সুক্ষকোন(ⅱ) ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 11 \times 12 \times \sin 68.67^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=61.48[/math]
 বর্গ একক[math]\text { (iii) } \frac{c}{\sin c}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\therefore R=\frac{13}{2 \times \sin 68.67^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=7.39^{\circ} \approx 7[/math]


Explanation:

Question #306 (ID: 473555)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এর [math]\angle B=40^{\circ}, \mathrm{a}=3 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{c}=7 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] হলে, ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ কত সে.মি.?

Options:
A. [math]4.3[/math]
B. [math]3.95[/math]
C. [math]6.5[/math]
D. [math]8.6[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos B=\frac{a^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}}{2 a c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}=a^{2}+c^{2}-2 a c \cos B[/math]
 [math]=9+49-2 \cdot 3 \cdot 7 \cdot \cos 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]b^{2}=25.83 \quad \therefore b=5.082[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{b}{\sin B}=2 R \Rightarrow R=[/math]
 [math]\frac{5.082}{2 \times \sin 40^{\circ}}=3.95 \text { (Ans:) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #307 (ID: 473556)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]\frac{1}{a} \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}+\frac{1}{b} \cos ^{2} \frac{B}{2}+\frac{1}{c} \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{s^{2}}{a b c}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{s}{\sqrt{a b c}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3 \mathrm{~s}^{2}}{\mathrm{abc}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3} \mathrm{~s}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{abc}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\left(\frac{1}{a} \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}+\frac{1}{b} \cos ^{2} \frac{B}{2}+\frac{1}{c} \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{a} \cdot \frac{S(s-a)}{b c}+\frac{1}{b} \cdot \frac{S(s-b)}{a c}+\frac{1}{c} \frac{s \cdot(s-c)}{a b}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{s(s-a)+s(s-b)+s(s-c)}{a b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{s^{2}-a s+s^{2}-b s+s^{2}-c s}{a b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 s^{2}-s(a+b+c)}{a b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 s^{2}-5.25}{a b c}=\frac{s^{2}}{a b c}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #308 (ID: 473557)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এর বাহুগুলো [math]4, 5[/math] ও [math]7[/math] একক হলে, এর অন্তঃবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ কত একক?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{\frac{3}{2}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math]
 এর অন্তঃবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 \Delta}{a+b+c} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sqrt{s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}}{a+b+c} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sqrt{8 \times(8-4) \times(8-5)(8-7)}}{16}=\sqrt{\frac{3}{2}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #311 (ID: 473560)

Question:
[math]\pi \leq \theta \leq \frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cot \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] হলে-

i. [math]\sin \theta=\frac{-4}{5}[/math]

ii. [math]\cos \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]

ii. [math]\tan 2 \theta=\frac{-24}{7}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{-4}{5} ; \cos \theta=\frac{-3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\tan 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cdot \frac{4}{3} .}{1-\left(\frac{4}{3}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{8}{3}}{\frac{9-16}{9}}=\frac{3.8}{-7}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{24}{7}[/math]

Question #313 (ID: 473562)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan A-\cot A=a[/math] এবং [math]\sin A-\cos A=b[/math] হলে-

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. } \cot 2 \mathrm{~A}=-\frac{\mathrm{a}}{2}\\\text{ii. } \sin 2 \mathrm{~A}=1-\mathrm{b}^{2}\\\text{iii. } \frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}=-\frac{a}{2}\left(1-b^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\text{(i) } \tan A-\frac{1}{\tan A}=\mathrm{a}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-1}{\tan \mathrm{A}}=\mathrm{a}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan ^{2} A-1}{2 \tan A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \tan A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{2}{a} \text{.}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan 2 A[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{2}{a}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot 2 A[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{a}{2}[/math]
 [math]\text{(ii) } \sin \mathrm{A}-\cos \mathbf{A}=\mathrm{b}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\sin ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} A-2 \sin A[/math]
 [math]\cos A=b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin A \cos A[/math]
 [math]=b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{b}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=1-\mathrm{b}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\text{(iii) } \sin 2 A=\frac{2 \tan A}{1+\tan ^{2} A},[/math]
 [math]\cot 2 A=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{2 \tan A}[/math]
 [math]\sin 2 A \cdot \cot 2 A[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{a}{2}\left(1-b^{2}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #314 (ID: 473563)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { ABC }[/math] সমকোণী ত্রিভুজে—

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. } \sin \mathrm{A}+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B\\\text{ii. } \cos A=\sin B-\cos C\\\text{iii. } \cos \mathrm{A}=\sin \mathrm{B}+\cos \mathrm{C}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. ii ও iii
গ. i ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\text { (ii) } \cos A=\sin B-\cos C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A+\cos C=\sin B .[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{A}{2}-\frac{B}{2}\right) \cdot \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=2 \cdot \sin \frac{B}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=\sin \frac{B}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\theta}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \quad \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=\cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{A-C}{2}=B / 2 \\\Rightarrow A-C=B \\\Rightarrow A=B+C \\\Rightarrow 2 A=A+B+C\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore A & =\frac{A+B+C}{L} \\& =\frac{\pi}{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
(iii)[math]\downarrow[/math]
(ii)-এর অনুরূপ।

Explanation:

Question #318 (ID: 473545)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{2}{3}[/math] এবং [math]\tan \alpha=\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin 2 \theta: \cos 2 \alpha[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]13: 15[/math]
B. [math]12: 15[/math]
C. [math]15: 13[/math]
D. [math]15: 12[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{2}{3}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\therefore \sin 2 \theta=2 \sin \theta \cdot \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2 \cdot \frac{2}{\sqrt{13}} \cdot \frac{3}{\sqrt{13}} \\=\frac{12}{13}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\cos ^{2} \alpha \\=\cos ^{2} \alpha-\sin ^{2} \alpha \\=\left(\frac{3}{\sqrt{10}}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{10}}\right)^{2} \\=\frac{9}{10}-\frac{1}{10}=\frac{4}{5}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 2 \theta: \cos 2 \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{12}{13}: \frac{4}{5} \\=\frac{3}{13}: \frac{1}{5}=15: 13\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cos ^{2}(x+y)+\cos ^{2}(x-y)-1[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি ?

Options:
ক. [math]\cos ^{2} 2 x-\sin ^{2} 2 y[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sin x \sin y[/math]
গ. [math]\cos 2 x \cos 2 y[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \cos x \cos y[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{2}(x+y)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2}(x-y)-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\left\{2 \cos ^{2}(x+y)+2 \cos ^{2}(x-y)\right\}-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\{1+\cos 2(x+y)+1+\cos 2(x-y)\}-1[/math]
 [math]=1+\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\{\cos 2(x+y)+\cos 2(x-y)\}-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \frac{2 x+2 y+2 x-2 y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{2 x+2 y-2 x+2 y}{2}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \cos C+\cos D=2 \cdot \cos \frac{c t D}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{c-D}{2}\right.[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 x \cdot \cos 2 y[/math]

D. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin 2 A=\frac{3}{5}=\frac{2 \tan A}{1+\tan ^{2} A} \\\Rightarrow 3+3 \tan ^{2} A=10 \tan A \\\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} A-10 \tan A+3=0 \\\therefore \tan A=3, \frac{1}{3}\end{array}[/math]

Question #324 (ID: 473551)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]\sec (A+B)[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\cos C[/math]
B. [math]\mathrm{secC}[/math]
C. [math]-\cos C[/math]
D. [math]-\operatorname{secC}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\angle A+\angle B+\angle C=\pi[/math]
 [math]\sec (A+B)=\sec (\pi-C)=-\sec C[/math]

Question #326 (ID: 473553)

Question:
[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{C}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি? (যখন [math]\mathbf{A}+\mathbf{B}+ \mathbf{C}=\pi)[/math]

Options:
A. [math]1-2 \cos A \cos B \sin C[/math]
B. [math]1-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \sin \mathrm{B} \sin \mathrm{C}[/math]
C. [math]1-2 \sin A \sin B \cos C[/math]
D. [math]1-2 \sin \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos C[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} A+2\cos ^{2} B\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(1+\cos 2 A+\cos ^{2} B+1\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(2+\cos 2 A+\cos ^{2} B\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]1+\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 A+\cos 2 B)+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]1+\frac{1}{2} 2 \cos (A+B) \cdot \cos (A-B)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]1+\frac{1}{2}\cos (\pi-C)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos (A-B)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=1-\cos C \cdot[/math]
 [math]\cos (A-B)+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=1-\cos[/math]
 [math]C[\cos (A-B)-\cos \{(\pi-(A+B)\}][/math]
 [math]=1-\cos C \cdot[/math]
 [math]\{\cos (A-B)-\cos (A+B)\}[/math]
 [math]=1-\cos C \cdot 2[/math]
 [math]\sin A \cdot \sin B[/math]
 [math]=1-2 \sin A \cdot[/math]
 [math]\sin B \cdot \cos C[/math]


Explanation:

Question #327 (ID: 473528)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


[math]\text { ABC }[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{8}{15}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{15}{17}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{8}{17}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{8}{15}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}(2 p+1)^{2}=(2 p-1)^{2}+p^{2} \\\Rightarrow(2 p+1)^{2}-(2 p-1)^{2}=p^{2} \\\Rightarrow 4 \cdot 2 p \cdot 1=p^{2} \\\Rightarrow p^{2}-8 p=0 \\\Rightarrow p(p-8)=0 \\\therefore p=8 ;[p 
eq 0] \\\therefore \cos \theta=\frac{p}{2 p+1}=\frac{8}{17}\end{array}[/math]

Question #329 (ID: 473530)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\cos A=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}, \cos B=\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\sin (A+B)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1+\sqrt{6}}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1-\sqrt{6}}{6}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1+2 \sqrt{6}}{6}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1-2 \sqrt{6}}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin A=\frac{\sqrt{2^{2}-(\sqrt{3})^{2}}}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{4-3}}{2}=\frac{1}{2} \\\sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3^{2}-1}}{3}=\frac{\sqrt{8}}{3}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{3} \\\therefore \sin (A+B)=\sin A \cos B+\cos A \sin B \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{1}{3}+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cdot \frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{3} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{6}+\frac{\sqrt{6}}{3}=\frac{1+2 \sqrt{6}}{6}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]A=45^{\circ}, B=30^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\sec (\mathbf{B}-\mathbf{A})[/math] এর মান কত?

B. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}+1}[/math]

 [math]\Rightarrow \cos 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cos 30^{\circ}+[/math]
 [math]\sin 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec (B-A)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}+1}[/math]

Question:
[math]\cot 4 \theta-\cot 2 \theta[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\sin 4 \theta[/math]
B. [math]\operatorname{cosec} 4 \theta[/math]
C. [math]-\cos 4 \theta[/math]
D. [math]-\operatorname{cosec} 4 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cos 4 \theta}{\sin 4 \theta}-\frac{\cos 2 \theta}{\sin 2 \theta} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 4 \theta \sin 2 \theta-\sin 4 \theta \cdot \cos 2 \theta}{\sin 4 \theta \cdot \sin 2 \theta} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin (-2 \theta)}{\sin 4 \theta \cdot \sin 2 \theta}=-\operatorname{cosec} 4 \theta\end{array}[/math]

Question:
[math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan A \cdot \tan B=1[/math] হলে, [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{8}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan A+\tan B=1-\tan A \cdot \tan B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \cdot \tan B}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan (A+B)=\tan \pi / 4[/math]
 [math]=A+B=\pi / 4[/math]


Explanation:

Question #334 (ID: 473535)

Question:
[math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+B\right) \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-B\right)[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\operatorname{Cos} B[/math]
B. [math]\operatorname{Sin} B[/math]
C. [math]0[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+B\right) \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-B\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}+\tan B}{1-\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \cdot \tan B} \cdot \frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}-\tan B}{1+\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \tan B} \\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{1+\tan B}{1-\tan B}\right)\left(\frac{1-\tan B}{1+\tan B}\right)=1\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #336 (ID: 473537)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\sin (A+B)=\frac{a}{b}[/math] এবং [math]\sin (\mathbf{A}-\mathbf{B})=\frac{\mathbf{b}}{\mathbf{a}}[/math] হলে, [math]\tan A \cot B[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a 2+b 2}{a 2-b 2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a 2-b 2}{a 2+b 2}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin (A+B)=\frac{a}{b}[/math]
 এবং [math]\sin (A-B)=\frac{b}{a}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{\sin (A+B)}{\sin (A-B)}=\frac{a^{2}}{b^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin (A+B)+\sin (A-B)}{\sin (A+B)-\sin (A-B)}=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{a^{2}-b^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin A \cos B}{2 \cdot \sin B \cdot \cos A}=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{a^{2}-b^{2}} \\\therefore\tan A \cdot \cot B=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{a^{2}-b^{2}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #337 (ID: 473538)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cot \left(\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cot \left(\frac{\beta-\alpha}{2}\right)=\frac{n}{n-2}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos \alpha[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]n \cos \beta[/math]
B. [math]n^{2} \cos \beta[/math]
C. [math](n-1) \cos \beta[/math]
D. [math](n+1) \cos \beta[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cot \left(\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cot \left(\frac{\beta-\alpha}{2}\right)=\frac{n}{n-2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{\beta-\alpha}{2}\right)}{2 \cdot \sin \left(\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \sin \left(\frac{\beta-\alpha}{2}\right)}=\frac{n}{n-2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \alpha+\cos \beta}{\cos \alpha-\cos \beta}=\frac{n}{n-2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \alpha+\cos \beta+\cos \alpha-\cos \beta}{\cos \alpha+\cos \beta-\cos \alpha+\cos \beta}=\frac{n+n-2}{n-n+2} ;\end{array}[/math]
[যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \alpha}{\cos \beta}=\frac{2 n-2}{2} \\\therefore \cos \alpha=(n-1) \cos \beta\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #338 (ID: 473539)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
