Question:
[math]2 \sin A+3 \cos A=3[/math] [math]\cos B+2 \sin B[/math] হলে [math]A + B[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]2 \tan ^{-1} \frac{2}{3}[/math]
B. [math]\tan ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math]
C. [math]2 \tan ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\cot ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]2 \sin A+3 \cos A=3 \cos B+2 \sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2(\sin A-\sin B)[/math]
 [math]=3(\cos B-\cos A)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cdot 2 \cdot \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{A+B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \cdot 2 \cdot \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+B}{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 \cdot \sin \frac{A+B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \left(\frac{A+B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B=2[/math]
 [math]\tan ^{-1}\left(\frac{2}{3}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

 [math]=\sin (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\sin (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin (A+B) \sin \left(90^{\circ}-\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}\right) ;[/math]
 [math]\left[\because A+B=90^{\circ}-\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \cdot 2[/math]
 [math]\sin (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sin 2(\mathrm{~A}+\mathrm{B})[/math]

Question #344 (ID: 473526)

Question:
[math]\cot \theta=\frac{-5}{12}[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta[/math] ঋণাত্মক হলে [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{12}{13}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{5}{13}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{12}{13}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cot \theta=-\frac{5}{12}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\therefore \cos \theta=\frac{5}{13}[/math]

B. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]

D. [math]-6[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

[Image]

 [math]=\frac{\tan \theta+\sec \theta}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-\frac{4}{3}-5 / 3}{-\frac{3}{4}-5 / 4}=3 / 2[/math]

Question #352 (ID: 473508)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2007-2008 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] হলে নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math]\sin \theta=-3 / 5 \text { and } \cos \theta=4 / 5[/math]
খ. [math]\sin \theta=3 / 5 \text { and } \cos \theta=-4 / 5[/math]
গ. [math]\sin \theta=-3 / 5 \text { and } \cos \theta=-4 / 5[/math]
ঘ. কোনটিই নয়।


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]1^{st}[/math]
 Quadrant এর ক্ষেত্রে [math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}, \sin \theta=3 / 5, \quad \cos \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]3^{rd}[/math]
 Quadrant এর ক্ষেত্রে [math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}, \sin \theta=-3 / 5, \quad \cos \theta=-4 / 5[/math]


Explanation:
[math]1^{st}[/math] Quadrant-এ সকল ত্রিকোণমিতিক অনুপাতের মান Positive । কিন্তু কোনো Option-এ একইসাথে sin, cos Positive নেই। আবার ওখ Quadrant-এ tan Positive কিন্তু sin cos Negative (C) Option-এ একইসাথে sin ও cos negative হওয়ায় সেটিই সঠিক উত্তর। মনে রাখবে, চারটি চতুর্ভাগের মাঝে ১ম চতুর্ভাগে সকল ত্রিকোণমিতিক অনুপাতের মান ধনাত্মক। ২য় চতুর্ভাগে শুধুমাত্র sin ও cosec ধনাত্মক, ৩য় চতুর্ভাগে শুধুমাত্র tan ও cot ধনাত্মক আর ৪র্থ চতুর্ভাগে cos ও secধনাত্মক।নিচের চিত্রটি দেখে মনে রাখতে পারো:

Question #353 (ID: 473509)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2007-2008 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
সমাধান কর: [math]\sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\cos \theta<\sqrt{3}, 0<\theta<\pi / 2[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\theta>\pi / 3[/math]
B. [math]\theta<\pi / 6[/math]
C. [math]\theta>\pi / 6[/math]
D. [math]\theta<\pi / 3[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { } \sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\cos \theta<\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{2} \cos \theta<\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta \cos \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]+\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \cos \theta<\sin \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(0+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)<\sin \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta+\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]<\mathrm{n} \pi+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta<\mathrm{n}[/math]
 [math]\pi+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{3}-\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]if \ , \mathrm{n}=0 \text { }[/math]
 [math]\theta<0+\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]-\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta<\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:
পাঠ্য বইতে সমীকরণের মাধ্যমে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর মান বের করার পদ্ধতি আলোকপাত করা হয়েছে। উক্ত প্রশ্নে অসমতার মাধ্যমে এর মান বের করতে হবে। শুধু সমান চিহ্ন না দিয়ে অসমতার মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ করলেই [math]\theta[/math]
 ও [math]\pi[/math]
 এর মাঝে সম্পর্ক পাওয়া যাবে।

Question #354 (ID: 473510)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2007-2008 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] কোন ত্রিভুজ [math]\frac{1}{a+c}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math] হলে, [math]\angle \mathrm{C}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]22.5^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{a+c}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{a+b+2 c}{a b+c a+b c+c^{2}}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{2}+a b+c a+a b+b^{2}+b c+2 c a+2 b c+2 c^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 a b+3 c a+3 b c+3 c^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}[/math]
 [math]=a b[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a b}{2 a b}=\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #355 (ID: 473511)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2007-2008 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের বাহুদ্বয় [math]\mathbf{B C}=\mathbf{a}, \mathbf{C A}=\mathbf{b}, \mathbf{A B}=\mathbf{c}[/math] হয় এবং [math](b+c-a)[/math] [math](a+b+c)=(\sqrt{3}+2) b c[/math] হয়, তবে A এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
D. কোনোটিই নয়


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](b+c-a)(a+b+c)=(\sqrt{3}+2) b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} b c+2 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=30^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #356 (ID: 473512)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Question:
[math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\tan A \tan B \tan C[/math] হলে, [math](A+B+C)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]\pi[/math]
D. [math]2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

 [math]=\frac{-(\tan A+\tan B)}{1-\tan A \cdot \tan B}[/math]
 [math]=-\tan (A+B)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \{\pi-(A+B)\}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C[/math]
 [math]=\pi-(A+B)[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B+C[/math]
 [math]=\pi[/math]

Question #360 (ID: 473488)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
[math]\cos 198^{\circ}+\sin 432^{\circ}+\tan 12^{\circ}+\tan 168^{\circ}[/math] এর মান

Options:
A. 0
B. -1
C. 1
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos 198^{\circ}+\sin 432^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 168^{\circ}+\tan 12^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 198^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin \left\{7 \times 90^{\circ}-198^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan \left\{180^{\circ}-12^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 198^{\circ}-\cos 198^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}-\tan 12=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
যদি [math]3 \sec ^{4} \theta+8=10 \sec ^{2} \theta[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
B. [math]\pm 1[/math]
C. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}, \pm 1[/math]
D. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}, \pm 1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]3 \sec ^{4} \theta+8-10 \sec ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3\left(1+\tan ^{2} \theta\right)^{2}+8-10-10 \tan ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3+6 \tan ^{2} \theta+3 \tan ^{4} \theta-2-10 \tan ^{2} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{4} \theta-3 \tan ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta+1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)-1\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(3 \tan ^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta=[/math]
 [math]\pm 1, \tan \theta=[/math]
 [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]

Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math] বর্গ সে.মি. এবং উহার দুই বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]3[/math] সে.মি. এবং [math]5[/math] সে.মি. উক্ত বাহু দুইটির অন্তর্গত কোণ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]135^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\Delta=\frac{1}{2} a b \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 3[/math]
 [math]\times 5 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]

Question:
একটি স্থুলকোণী ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলোর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]3 \mathrm{~cm}, 5 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] ও [math]7 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] হলে স্থুলকোণটি কত?

Options:
ক. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]135^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]100[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
বাহুগুলোর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]3cm, 5cm[/math]
 এবং [math]7 cm[/math]
.যদি স্থুলকোণ [math]A[/math]
 হয় তবে, [math]\cos A=\frac{3^{2}+5^{2}-7^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5} \therefore A=120^{\circ}[/math]
 [বৃহত্তম বাহুর বিপরীত কোণ বৃহত্তম ]।

Question #372 (ID: 473500)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=x[/math] হয় তবে [math]\sin \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{x+1}{x-1}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{x-1}{x+1}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{x^{2}+1}{x^{2}-1}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি থেকে একবার tan θ এর মান বের করো, আবার sece এর মান বের করো। এরপর tan θ কে sec θ দ্বারা ভাগ করলেই sin θ এর মান পেয়ে যাবে।[math]\\[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{Solve: } \tan \theta+\sec \theta=x \\\Rightarrow \sec \theta=x-\tan \theta\\\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=x^{2}-2 x \tan \theta+\tan ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow 1+\tan ^{2} \theta=x^{2}-2 x \tan \theta+\tan ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{2 x}\end{array}[/math]
আবার, (i) নং সমীকরণ থেকে,[math]\sec \theta=x-\tan \theta=x-\frac{x^{2}-1}{2 x}=\frac{x^{2}+1}{2 x}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{\tan \theta}{\sec \theta}=\sin \theta=\frac{x^{2}-1}{2 x} \times \frac{2 x}{x^{2}+1}=\frac{x^{2}-1}{x^{2}+1}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি দেখে সহজেই বুঝা যায়, এখান থেকে tan θ ও sec θ এর মান আলাদা আলাদাভাবে বের করা সম্ভব। এক্ষেত্রে তা-ই করা হয়েছে।আর, [math]\frac{\tan \theta}{\sec \theta}==\frac{\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}}{\frac{1}{\cos \theta}}=\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta} \times \frac{\cos \theta}{1}=\sin \theta[/math]অর্থাৎ tan θ কে sec θ দ্বারা ভাগ করলে sin θ পাওয়া যায়। তাই এরপর sine এর মান পাওয়ার জন্য tan θ কে sec θ দ্বারা ভাগ করা হয়েছে।

Sub-Questions:

Question #373 (ID: 473501)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos x+\sqrt{3} \sin x=\sqrt{2}[/math] সমীকরণের সমাধান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \mathrm{n} \pi+\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \mathrm{n} \pi+\frac{7 \pi}{12}[/math]
গ. [math]2 \mathrm{n} \pi+\frac{ \pi}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{Hints:}\\\text{- } \sin A \sin B+\cos A \cos B=\cos (A-B)\\\text{- } \cos \theta=\cos \alpha \\\Rightarrow \text{ } \theta=2 n \pi \pm \alpha\\\text{Solve: } \cos x+\sqrt{3} \sin x=\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \cos x+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \sin x=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\pi}{3} \cos x+\sin \frac{\pi}{3} \sin x=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \\\Rightarrow \cos \left(x-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\cos \frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow x-\frac{\pi}{3}=2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow x=2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{\pi}{3} \\\therefore x=2 n \pi+\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{\pi}{3}=2 n \pi+\frac{7 \pi}{12} \\\text { and } x=2 n \pi-\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{\pi}{3}=2 n \pi+\frac{\pi}{12}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\cos x+\sqrt{3} \sin x=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 আকারের সমীকরণকে সূত্রের সাথে মিলানোর জন্য সমীকরণটির উভয়পাশে cosx ও sinx এর সহগের বর্গের যোগফলের বর্গমূল দিয়ে ভাগ করতে হবে।এক্ষেত্রে COSx এর সহগ l ও sinx এর সহগ √3তাহলে এদের সহগের বর্গের যোগফলের বর্গমূল [math]=\sqrt{1^{2}+(\sqrt{3})^{2}}=\sqrt{4}=2[/math]
By Calculator: অপশনে n = (0) কিংবা 1 ধরে x এর মান অপশন থেকে বসাবে। প্রশ্নের সমীকরণের বামপক্ষটুকু ক্যালকুলেটরে তুলে x এর যে মানের জন্য সমীকরণটির মান √2 আসবে, সেটাই সমীকরণটির সমাধান।

Question #374 (ID: 473502)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\cos \theta[/math] এর সর্বোচ্চ মান কত?

Options:
A. √3+1
B. 2
C. √3
D. √3-1


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: sin [math]\theta[/math]
 = 1 বা cos θ = 1 এর জন্য মান সর্বোচ্চ হবে। এক্ষেত্রে sin θ ও cos θ দুটি অনুপাতকে যেকোন একটি অনুপাতে রূপান্তর করতে হবে।[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { Solve: } \sqrt{3} \sin \theta+\cos \theta=2\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \cos \theta\right) \\=2\left(\sin \theta \cos \frac{\pi}{6}+\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \cos \theta\right) \\=2 \sin \left(\theta+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=2 \times 1=2\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যাঃ এখানে sinA cosB + cosA sinB = sin (A+B) এর ফর্মুলা ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে। sin (A+B) = 1 এর জন্য সর্বোচ্চ মান পাওয়া যায় ।

Sub-Questions:

Question #375 (ID: 473503)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a = 8, b = 4[/math] এবং [math]c = 6[/math] হলে, [math]\angle A =?[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\sin ^{-1}\left(\sqrt{\frac{5}{8}}\right)[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sin ^{-1}\left(\sqrt{\frac{5}{8}}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\cos ^{-1}(4 / 5)[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{4}{5}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Hints: } \sin \frac{A}{2}=\sqrt{\frac{(s-b)(s-c)}{b c}} \ \ \ \ \ \ \text {; }[/math]
 যেখানে s হচ্ছে অর্ধপরিসীমা ।[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { Solve: } s=\frac{8+4+6}{2}=9 \\\sin \frac{A}{2}=\sqrt{\frac{(9-4)(9-6)}{4 \times 6}}=\sqrt{\frac{5 \times 3}{4 \times 6}}=\sqrt{\frac{5}{8}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{A}{2}=\sin ^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{5}{8}} \\\Rightarrow A=2 \sin ^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{5}{8}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: Option এ [math]sin^{-1}[/math]
 দ্বারা উত্তর করা আছে তাই A কোণের মান বের করার সময় sin সম্বলিত সূত্র ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে। Option অনুযায়ী আমাদের উত্তরের ক্ষেত্রে কোন সূত্র ব্যবহার করব তা ঠিক করতে হবে। এজন্য কোণের ক্ষেত্রে পাঠ্যবইয়ের সবধরনের সূত্র সম্পর্কে ধারণা থাকা উচিত।বিকল্প নিয়ম: অঙ্কটি Cosine Rule দিয়েও করতে পারো ।[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}=\frac{4^{2}+6^{2}-8^{2}}{2.4 .6}=\frac{-12}{48}=-\frac{1}{4} \\\therefore A=\cos ^{-1}\left(-\frac{1}{4}\right)=104.47^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, (B) Option থেকে [math]2 \sin ^{-1}\left(\sqrt{\frac{5}{8}}\right)=104.47^{\circ}[/math]
অর্থাৎ Ans. হচ্ছে (B)

Question #376 (ID: 473504)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
ABC একটি সমদ্বিবাহু ত্রিভুজ যার a = 10√2 cm এবং b = c ত্রিভুজটির পরিলিখিত বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ 10 cm হলে [math]\angle B =?[/math]

Options:
ক. 75°
খ. 67.5°
গ. 15°
ঘ. 22.5°


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Hints: } \frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 এখানে R = পরিব্যাসার্ধ।[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { Solve: } \frac{a}{\sin A}=2 \mathrm{R} \Rightarrow \frac{10 \sqrt{2}}{\sin A}=2 \times 10 \Rightarrow \mathrm{A}=45^{\circ} \\\mathrm{b}=\mathrm{c} \text { হলে} \angle \mathrm{B}=\angle \mathrm{C}\\ \text { এখন, } \angle \mathrm{A}+\angle \mathrm{B}+\angle \mathrm{C}=180^{\circ} \\=45^{\circ}+\angle \mathrm{B}+\angle \mathrm{B}=180^{\circ} \Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{B}=67.5^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: sin এর সূত্র ব্যবহার করে প্রথমে A কোণের মান বের করা হয়েছে। এরপর ত্রিভুজের দুটি বাহু সমান হলে বিপরীত কোণদ্বয় সমান হয় এই সূত্র ব্যবহার করে B = C বের করা হয়েছে।

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
ABC ত্রিভুজে [math]a = 5√2[/math] একক [math]b = 6[/math] একক [math]\angle A = 60°[/math] এবং [math]\angle B = 45°, C=?[/math]

Options:
A. 11
B. 8
C. 3(√3+1)
D. 6


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Hints: } C[/math]
 [math]=a \cos B+b \cos A[/math]
 [math]\text { Solve: } C=a[/math]
 [math]\cos B+b \cos A=5[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{2} \cos 45^{\circ}+6 \cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=5+3=8[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এখানে সূত্রে প্রদত্ত মানগুলো বসিয়ে দিয়ে C এর মান বের করা হয়েছে। অবশ্য sin এর সূত্র প্রয়োগ করেও মান বের করা যাবে। তবে এভাবে করলেই অঙ্কটা সহজ ও ছোট হয়। এ টাইপের অঙ্কের জন্য ত্রিভূজের ধর্মাবলী সংক্রান্ত সকল সূত্র আয়ত্ত্বে রাখা উচিত।

Question #378 (ID: 473506)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos ^{4} A-\sin ^{4} A[/math] এর মান নিম্নের কোনটির সমান হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \cos ^{2} A-1[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sin ^{2} A-1[/math]
গ. [math]2 \tan ^{2} A-1[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \sec ^{2} A-1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{4} A-\sin ^{4} A[/math]
 [math]=\left(\cos ^{2} A\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]-\left(\sin ^{2} A\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=1 \times \cos 2 \mathrm{~A}=2 \cos ^{2} A-1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #379 (ID: 473507)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] কোন ত্রিভুজে যদি [math]B+C=2 A[/math] হয়, তবে [math]2 a \cos \frac{B-C}{2}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ab}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
গ. [math]a+b[/math]
ঘ. [math]b+c[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]B+C=2 A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 180-A=2 A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\text{Now, } \frac{\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{a}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \mathrm{B}+\sin \mathrm{C}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin \frac{2 \mathrm{~A}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]=2 \operatorname{acos} \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \mathrm{a} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=(\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c})[/math]


Explanation:

Question #380 (ID: 473443)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের [math](\sqrt{3}+1) \mathrm{cm}[/math] দৈর্ঘ্য বিশিষ্ট বাহু সংলগ্ন দুটি কোন [math]30^{\circ}[/math] ও [math]45^{\circ}[/math] । ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math]1 / 2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
খ. [math]2[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt{3}+1)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\text { Non of these }[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
ত্রিভুজের [math]\text { sine }[/math]
 সূত্র মতে, [math]\frac{A B}{\sin 45^{\circ}}=\frac{(\sqrt{3}+1)}{\sin 105^{\circ}} \Rightarrow A B=\frac{(\sqrt{3}+1) \sin 45^{\circ}}{\sin \left(115^{\circ})\right.}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{AB}=2[/math]
 (ক্যালকুলেটর ব্যবহার করে)[math]\therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজ এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2}|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{BC}}|=\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{AB} \cdot \mathrm{BC} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\Rightarrow\frac{1}{2} \times 2 \times(\sqrt{3}+1) \times \frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt{3}+1)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #383 (ID: 473449)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের বাহুত্রয় [math]2 x+3, x^{2}+3 x+3[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+2 x[/math] - হলে বৃহত্তম কোণটি কত হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. কোনটিই নয়


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সবচেয়ে বড় বাহু [math]a=\left(x^{2}+3 x+3\right)[/math]
 এবং বড় কোন Aহলে, [math]\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(2 x+3)^{2}+\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)^{2}-\left(x^{2}+3 x+3\right)^{2}}{2 \times(2 x+3)\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}=120^{\circ} \text { [Shortcut, } \mathrm{x}=1[/math]
 হলে, [math]a=7, b=5, c=3[/math]
 [math]\left.\therefore \cos A=\frac{5^{2}+3^{2}-7^{2}}{2 \times 5 \times 3}\right][/math]


Explanation:

Question #386 (ID: 473452)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]g(\theta)=\frac{1-\tan \theta}{1+\tan \theta}[/math] হয় [math]g\left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right)[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sin \theta[/math]
B. [math]\cos \theta[/math]
C. [math]\tan \theta[/math]
D. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]g\left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right)=[/math]
 [math]\frac{1-\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right)}{1+\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}-\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right)}{1+\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\theta\right) \tan \frac{\pi}{4}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}-\frac{\pi}{4}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #387 (ID: 473453)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2\left(\cos ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=1[/math]; হলে [math]\theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
C. [math]n \pi+(-1)^{n} \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
D. কোনটিই নয়


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]2\left(\cos ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos (2 \theta)=1[/math]
 [math]\Leftrightarrow \cos (2 \theta)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \theta=2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta=n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #388 (ID: 473455)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cot A \cot B+\cot B \cot C+\cot C \cot A=1[/math] হলে, [math]\text { A, B }[/math] এবং [math]C[/math] এর মধ্যে সম্পর্ক কি?

Options:
A. [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi[/math]
B. [math]A+B+C=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]A+B+C=2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]A+B+C=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\text { or }; \cot \mathrm{A} \cot \mathrm{B}+\cot \mathrm{B} \cot \mathrm{C}+\cot \mathrm{C} \cot\mathrm{A}=1[/math]
 [math]\Leftrightarrow \cot \mathrm{A} \cot \mathrm{B}+\cot \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math](\cot \mathrm{B}+\cot \mathrm{A})=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cot A \cot B-1}{\cot B+\cot A}=[/math]
 [math]-\cot C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cot (A+B)=\cot (n \pi-C)[/math]
 [math];[n \in Z][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A+B=n \pi-C \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B+C=n \pi[/math]


Explanation:

একটি ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলোর পরিমাণ যথাক্রমে [math]3, 5[/math] এবং [math]7[/math] হলে ত্রিভুজটি কোন প্রকারের?

খ. সূক্ষ্মকোণী

ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষুদ্র দুই বাহুর জন্য, [math]\sqrt{3^{2}+5^{2}}=\sqrt{34}[/math] যা তৃতীয় বাহু অপেক্ষা ক্ষুদ্রতর। তাই ত্রিভুজটি স্থূলকোণী ।

Question #391 (ID: 473459)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]tan2x \ tanx = 1[/math] সমীকরণে [math]x[/math] এর কোন দুটি মান সঠিক নয়?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{7 \pi}{6}, \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{14 \pi}{6}, \frac{15 \pi}{6}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{8 \pi}{6}, \frac{9 \pi}{6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{13 \pi}{6}, \frac{11 \pi}{6}[/math]
ঙ. [math]\frac{19 \pi}{6}, \frac{17 \pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Hints: অপশনের যে মান দ্বারা [math]tan2x \ tanx = 1[/math]
 সমীকরণটি সিদ্ধ হবে না, সেগুলিই x এর সঠিক মান নয়।[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { Solve: } \tan 2 x \tan x=1 \Rightarrow \frac{2 \tan x}{1-\tan ^{2} x} \tan x=1 \\\quad \Rightarrow 2 \tan ^{2} x=1-\tan ^{2} x \Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} x=1 \Rightarrow \tan ^{2} x=\frac{1}{3} \\\Rightarrow \tan x= \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \tan x=\tan \left( \pm \frac{\pi}{6}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{x}=\mathrm{n} \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 যেখানে [math]\mathrm{n}=0, \pm 1, \pm 2 \ldots.[/math]
এখন n এর মান একটি একটি করে বসালে অপশন (C) বাদে বাকীগুলো পাওয়া যায়। অর্থাৎ (C) অপশনের মানগুলো সঠিক নয়।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যাঃ এ ধরনের ত্রিকোণমিতিক সমীকরণের সমাধান করার সময় Calculator ব্যবহার করে Option Test করে করবে। তাহলে ভুলের সম্ভাবনা কম থাকবে। আর মনে রাখবে, [math]\tan \theta=\tan \alpha[/math]
 হলে, [math]\theta=n \pi \pm \alpha[/math]
 [math]\\ \ \\[/math]
By Calculator: ক্যালকুলেটরে হুবহু [math]tan2x \ tanx[/math]
 ফাংশনটি Input দিবে। x ইনপুট দেয়ার জন্য Shift) বাটন দুটি চাপতে হবে। ফাংশনটি ইনপুট দেয়ার পর CALC বাটন চেপে x এর মান Option থেকে একটা একটা করে বসিয়ে = বাটন চেপে চেক করবে কোন মানগুলোর জন্য । আসে না। যেগুলির জন্য 1 আসবে না, সেগুলিই Ans.যদি সরাসরি x এর মান । [math]\pi[/math]
 আকারে Input দিতে চাও, তবে ক্যালকুলেটর Radian মুডে রাখতে হবে। আর Degree মুডে রাখলে কে 180 হিসেবে Input দিতে হবে।

Question #392 (ID: 473460)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]3 \sin ^{2} 30^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 30^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]0.5[/math]
B. [math]3/4[/math]
C. [math]0.25[/math]
D. [math]1.5[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]3 \sin ^{2} 30^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=3 \times\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{2}=1.5[/math]


Explanation:

Question #393 (ID: 473461)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
যদি [math]n[/math] এর মান জোড় হয়, তবে [math]\cos \theta+\cos (\pi+\theta)[/math] [math]+\cos (2 \pi+\theta)+\ldots[/math] [math]+\cos (n \pi+\theta)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\cos \theta[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]n \cos \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos n \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta+\cos (\pi+\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \theta-\cos \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\cos (2 \pi+\theta)+\cos (3 \pi+\theta)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \theta-\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
এখন, n জোড় হওয়ায় n এর আগেরটি বিজোড় হবে। বিজোড় পর্যন্ত মান 0 হবে। এখন শুধু বাদ থাকবে,[math]\cos (n \pi+\theta)=\cos \theta[/math]
 (n জোড় হওয়ায়)

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cos A=\frac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cos B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{4}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{1}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)=\cos ^{2} B-\cos ^{2} A[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}=\frac{1}{2}-\frac{1}{4}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #396 (ID: 473464)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question #398 (ID: 473466)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=m \cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=n \cos \theta[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\left(m^{2}-n^{2}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]4 \mathrm{mn}[/math]
B. [math]4 \sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]
D. [math]\mathrm{mn}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=m \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\sin \theta \cos \theta=m \cos \theta \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta+\sin \theta=m\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]m^{2}-n^{2}=(m+n)(m-n)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=4 \tan \theta \sin \theta=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)} \\=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta}=4 \sqrt{m n}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=n \cos \theta \\\therefore \tan \theta-\sin \theta=n \\m+n=2 \tan \theta \\m-n=2 \sin \theta \\m n=\tan ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{x}[/math], হলে [math]\sin 2 \theta=[/math] কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2 x}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1-x^{2}}{1+x^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2 x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin 2 \theta=\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{2 \cdot \frac{1}{x}}{1+\frac{1}{x^{2}}}=\frac{2 x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]

Question:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin A[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\tan \mathrm{A}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)[/math]
 [math]=\tan[/math]
 [math]A\left(1+\frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \mathrm{A}\left(\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+1+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \mathrm{A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]

Question:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin 2 \alpha[/math]
B. [math]\sin \alpha[/math]
C. [math]\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1-\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}{1+\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\cos 2\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+2 \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 2 \alpha[/math]

Question #402 (ID: 473470)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #403 (ID: 473471)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\cos x+\cos y=a[/math] এবং [math]\sin x+\sin y=b[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\cos (x+y)[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a-b}{a+b}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2 a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{a^{3}+2 b^{2}}{a^{3}-b^{2}}[/math]
E. [math]\frac{a^{2}+3 b^{2}}{a^{2}-2 b^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]a^{2}=\cos ^{2} x+\cos ^{2} y+2 \cos x \cdot \cos y ;[/math]
 [math]b^{2}=\sin ^{2} x+\sin ^{2} y+2 \sin x \cdot \sin y[/math]
 [math]\therefore a^{2}-b^{2}=[/math]
 [math]\cos 2 x+\cos 2 y+2 \cos (x+y) ;[/math]
 [math]a^{2}+b^{2}[/math]
 [math]=2+2 \cos (x-y)[/math]
এখন, [math]a^{2}-b^{2}=2 \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos (x-y)+2 \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\cos (x+y)\{2 \cos (x-y)+2\}[/math]
 [math]=\cos (x+y) \times\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #408 (ID: 473477)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University of Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { For the } \mathrm{ABC} \text { triangle, if } \cos \mathrm{A}=\sin \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{C} \text {, the angle } \mathrm{C} \text { is }-[/math]

Options:
A. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C[/math]
 [math]=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A-C=-B \Rightarrow A+B=C ;[/math]
 [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow C+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow C=90^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #411 (ID: 473480)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=m \cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]\theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=n \cos \theta[/math] হলে [math]m^{2}-n^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]4mn[/math]
B. [math]4 \sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{m n}[/math]
D. [math]1 / \sqrt{m n}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: এখানে m ও n কে একপাশে রেখে Equation দুটিকে সরল করে তারপর [math]m^{2}-n^{2}[/math]
 এর মান বের করতে হবে ।[math]\text { Solve: } \sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=m \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{2} \frac{2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}{\cos \theta}=m[/math]
 [math][\cos \theta[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta+\sin \theta=m[/math]
এবং [math]\sin \theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=n \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}-\frac{1}{2} \frac{2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=n[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{n}[/math]
 [math]\ldots \ldots . . { (ii) }[/math]
 [math]=\text { (i) })^{2}-(\mathrm{ii})^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{m}^{2}-\mathrm{n}^{2}[/math]
 [math]=(\tan \theta+\sin \theta)^{2}-(\tan \theta-\sin \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=4 \tan \theta \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)}[/math]
 [math]=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=4 \sqrt{(\tan \theta+\sin \theta)(\tan \theta-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=4 \sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রশ্নে যেহেতু [math]m^{2}-n^{2}[/math]
 এর মান বের করতে বলা হয়েছে, সেহেতু প্রশ্নের সমীকরণ দুটা থেকে প্রথমে m আর n কে Free করে নেয়া হয়েছে [math]\sin 2 \theta=2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
 এবং [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=1-\cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
 সূত্রদ্বয় ছাড়া আর = তেমন কোনো ত্রিকোণমিতিক সূত্রের প্রয়োজন পড়েনি।

 [math]\therefore A=45^{\circ}[/math]

Question:
যদি [math]\cot A \cot B+\cot B \cot C+\cot C \cot A=1[/math] 1 হয়, তবে [math]A+B+C[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\pi[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi \Rightarrow \cot (\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C})=\cot (\pi-\mathrm{A})[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cot B \cot C-1}{\cot B+\cot C}=-\cot A \\\therefore \cot B \cot C+\cot C \cot A+\cot A \cot B=1\end{array}[/math]

Question #416 (ID: 473485)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2009-2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta-\cos 7 \theta=\sin 4 \theta[/math] সমীকরণে θ এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{n \pi}{3}-\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{n \pi}{3}-\frac{\pi}{16}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{3}+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{18}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\mathrm{n} \pi}{3}+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\text { Hints: } \cos C-\cos D=2 \sin \frac{C+D}{2} \sin \frac{D-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\sin \theta=\sin \alpha[/math]
 হলে [math]\theta=\mathrm{n} \pi+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \propto,[/math]
 যেখানে [math]\mathrm{n} \in \mathrm{Z}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text { Solve: } \cos \theta-\cos 7 \theta=\sin 4 \theta \\\quad \Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\theta+7 \theta}{2} \sin \frac{7 \theta-\theta}{2}-\sin 4 \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin 4 \theta \sin 3 \theta-\sin 4 \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow \sin 4 \theta(2 \sin 3 \theta-1)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\ \\ \ \ \\ \\[/math]
হয়[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { } \sin 4 \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow 4 \theta=\mathrm{n} \pi \\\Rightarrow \theta=\mathrm{n} \frac{\pi}{4} ;[\mathrm{n} \in Z]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\ \ \\[/math]
অথবা[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{ } 2 \sin 3 \theta-1=0\\\Rightarrow \sin 3 \theta=\frac{1}{2}=\sin \frac{\pi}{6} \\\Rightarrow 3 \theta=\mathrm{n} \pi+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{6}[\mathrm{n} \in \mathrm{Z}] \\\Rightarrow \theta=\mathrm{n} \frac{\pi}{3}+(-1)^{\mathrm{n}} \frac{\pi}{18}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: Solve অংশে 8 এর দুটি মান বের হয়েছে, কিন্তু Option-এ একটি দেওয়া আছে। Option Test করেও অংকটি করতে পারো। সেক্ষেত্রে অপশন থেকে B এর মান বসিয়ে সমীকরণটির বামপক্ষ ও ডানপক্ষ ক্যালকুলেটরের সাহায্যে মিলাতে হবে।

Question:
যদি, [math]\tan \theta=\frac{5}{12}[/math] এবং [math]\cos \theta[/math] ধনাত্মক হয়, তবে [math]\frac{\sin \theta+\cos (-\theta)}{\sec (-\theta)+\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{34}{39}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{34}{40}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{30}{39}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{35}{50}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{5}{12} ; \cos \theta=\frac{12}{13} ; \sin \theta=\frac{5}{13} \mid \theta[/math]
 কোনটি ১ম চতুর্ভাগে অবস্থিত।[math]\therefore \frac{\sin \theta+\cos (-\theta)}{\sec (-\theta)+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}{\sec \theta+\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{5}{13}+\frac{12}{13}}{\frac{13}{12}+\frac{5}{12}}=\frac{17}{13}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{12}{18}=\frac{34}{39}[/math]

Question #419 (ID: 473438)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019, 2014-2015, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \tan 40^{\circ} \tan 80^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
D. [math]-\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{2 \sin 80^{\circ} \sin 40^{\circ}}{2 \cos 80^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}-\cos 120^{\circ}}{\cos 40^{\circ}+\cos 120^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2}}{\cos 40^{\circ}-\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ}+1}{2 \cos 40^{\circ}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}-\sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ}+\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 60}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #420 (ID: 473440)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\cos x+\cos y=a[/math] এবং [math]\sin x+\sin y=b[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\cos (x+y)[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a-b}{a+b}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2 a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{a^{3}+2 b^{2}}{a^{3}-b^{2}}[/math]
E. [math]\frac{a^{2}+3 b^{2}}{a^{2}-2 b^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]a^{2}=\cos ^{2} x+\cos ^{2} y+2 \cos x \cdot \cos y ;[/math]
 [math]b^{2}=\sin ^{2} x+\sin ^{2} y+2 \sin x \cdot \sin y[/math]
 [math]\therefore a^{2}-b^{2}=[/math]
 [math]\cos 2 x+\cos 2 y+2 \cos (x+y) ;[/math]
 [math]a^{2}+b^{2}[/math]
 [math]=2+2 \cos (x-y)[/math]
এখন, [math]a^{2}-b^{2}=2 \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos (x-y)+2 \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\cos (x+y)\{2 \cos (x-y)+2\}[/math]
 [math]=\cos (x+y) \times\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (x+y)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

E. [math]1[/math]

 [math]B=\sin ^{2} B-\sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]A=\sin (B+A) \cdot \sin (B-A)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow1 \cdot \sin (B-A)[/math]
 [math]\left[\because(A+B)=\frac{\pi}{2}\right][/math]
 [math]=\sin (B-A)[/math]

Question #423 (ID: 473419)

Question:
[math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\tan x[/math]
B. [math]\cos x[/math]
C. [math]\sec x[/math]
D. [math]\sin x[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2 x)}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2 \times 2 \cos ^{2} 2 x}}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+2 \cos 2 x}} \\=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2 x)}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} x}}=\frac{2}{2 \cos x}=\sec x\end{array}[/math]

Question #426 (ID: 473422)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Pabna University of Science and Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta(1+\sec 2 \theta)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\cot 2 \theta[/math]
B. [math]\tan 2 \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sec 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta(1+\sec 2 \theta)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan \theta\left(1+\frac{1}{\cos 2 \theta}\right) \\=\tan \theta\left(\frac{1+\cos 2 \theta}{\cos ^{2} \theta}\right) \\=\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta} \times \frac{2 \cos ^{2} \theta}{\cos 2 \theta} \\=\frac{2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}{\cos 2 \theta} \\=\frac{\sin 2 \theta}{\cos 2 \theta}=\tan 2 \theta\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #431 (ID: 473433)

Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]b^{2} \sin 2 C+c^{2} \sin 2 B[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]4 \Delta[/math]
B. [math]\Delta[/math]
C. [math]2 \Delta[/math]
D. [math]None[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}=2 b^{2} \sin C \cos C+2 c^{2} \sin B \cos B \\=2 b^{2} \frac{c}{2 R} \cos C+2 c^{2} \frac{b}{2 R} \cos B \\=\frac{b c}{R}(b \cos C+c \cos B)=\frac{a b c}{R}=4 \Delta\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #432 (ID: 473434)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]\angle B=55^{\circ}, \angle C=80^{\circ}, a=20 \sqrt{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math] হলে, ত্রিভুজটির পরিলিখিত বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ কত [math]cm[/math] হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]10[/math]
খ. [math]10 \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]20[/math]
ঘ. [math]20 \sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\angle \mathrm{A}=180^{\circ}-\left(55^{\circ}+80^{\circ}\right)=45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=2 R \Rightarrow \frac{20 \sqrt{2}}{\sin 45^{\circ}}=2 R \therefore R=20 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #433 (ID: 473386)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]-\frac{\pi}{2} [math]tanx – 3x = 0[/math] এর কয়টি মূল আছে?

Options:
ক. 0
খ. 1
গ. 2
ঘ. 3
ঙ. 4


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
Hints: ফাংশনটির ত্রিকোণমিতিক লেখচিত্র এঁকে সেখান থেকে মূল বের করতে পারো।Solve: [math]tanx – 3x = 0; y = tanx[/math]
 এবং [math]y = 3x[/math]
 এর জন্য লেখচিত্র আঁকলে ফাংশনন্বয়ের ছেদবিন্দুই হবে [math]tanx 3x = 0[/math]
 সমীকরণের সমাধান। উক্ত লেখচিত্রের ছেদবিন্দু তিনটি (A, O, B বিন্দু)। ফলে সমাধান তিনটি।

Explanation:


[math]y = tanx[/math]
 ও y = 3x অর্থাৎ [math]tanx = 3x[/math]
 বা [math]tanx - 3x = 0[/math]
 সমীকরণটির লেখচিত্রটি পাশের চিত্রে অঙ্কন করা হয়েছে। লেখচিত্রে দেখা যাচ্ছে,[math]-\pi / 2[/math]
 থেকে [math]\pi / 2[/math]
 রেঞ্জের ভিতর [math]y = 3x[/math]
 রেখাটি ছেদ করে। বিন্দু তিনটি হচ্ছে, A, O ও By = tanx কে তিনটি বিন্দুতেঅর্থাৎ সমীকরণটির তিনটি সমাধান বিদ্যমান

Question #436 (ID: 473389)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #437 (ID: 473390)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011, 2022-2023, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #438 (ID: 473391)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #440 (ID: 473393)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Textiles, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\tan \alpha-\tan \beta=p, \cot \beta-\cot \alpha=q, \alpha-\beta=\theta[/math] হয় তবে [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{p}-\frac{1}{q}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{q}-\frac{1}{p}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
D. [math]1-\frac{p}{q}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{p}=\tan \alpha-\tan \beta=\frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}-\frac{\sin \beta}{\cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\sin \beta \cos \alpha}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{p}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}[/math]
 [math]q=\cot \beta-\cot \alpha=\frac{\cos \beta}{\sin \beta}-\frac{\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\cos \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}=\cot (\alpha-\beta) ;[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
n পূর্ণ সংখ্যা হলে, [math]\cos \left\{(2 n+1) \pi+\frac{\pi}{3}\right\}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos \left(x-45^{\circ}\right)=\cos x \cos 45^{\circ}+\sin x \sin 45^{\circ} \\=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos x+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin x=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}(\cos x+\sin x)\end{array}[/math]

Question #442 (ID: 473395)

Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{a \cos \varphi-b}{a-b \cos \varphi}[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{\tan \frac{\theta}{2}}{\tan \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a+b \sin \varphi}{b+a \sin \varphi}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{\frac{a+b \cos \varphi}{a-b \sin \varphi}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\frac{a+b}{a-b}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{(a+b)^{2}}{a-b}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{a \cos \varphi-b}{a-b \cos \varphi}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(a+b)(1-\cos \varphi)}{(a-b)(1+\cos \varphi)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a+b}{a-b}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\tan \frac{\theta}{2}}{\tan \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{a+b}{a-b}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #443 (ID: 473396)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]+\sin \beta=\mathbf{a}[/math] এবং [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=b[/math] হয়, তাহলে [math]\cos (\alpha-\beta)[/math] এর মান কত? [

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}+2}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-2}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}-2}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}+2}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \alpha+\sin \beta[/math]
 [math]=a \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=b \ldots \text {(ii)}[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) }{ }^{2}+(\mathrm{ii})^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+1+2 \sin \alpha \sin \beta+2 \cos \alpha \cos \beta[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2(\cos \alpha \cos \beta+\sin \alpha \cos \beta)[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos (\alpha \beta)=\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-2[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (\alpha\beta)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-2}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #445 (ID: 473398)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]A+B+C=\pi \theta^{B} \cos A+\cos B=\sin C[/math] হয় তবে [math]B[/math] কোণের মান হলে-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos B+\cos A[/math]
 [math]=\sin C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos\frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{c}}{2} \cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}=\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #446 (ID: 473399)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\sin \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=2[/math] হয় ,তবে [math]\sin ^{n}\theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} \theta[/math] এর মান হলো-

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]-1[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]-2[/math]
E. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+1=2 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+1-2 \sin \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sin \theta-1)^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\text{Now, } \sin ^{n} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} 0[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{n} \theta+\frac{1}{\sin ^{n} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=(1)^{n}+\frac{1}{(1)^{n}}[/math]
 [math]=1+1=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question #447 (ID: 473400)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \cos \alpha\right)=\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \sin \alpha\right)[/math] হয় ,তবে [math]\alpha[/math] এর মান হলো-

Options:
A. [math]0, \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}, \frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]0, \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
E. [math]-\frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \cos \alpha\right)=\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \sin \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \cos \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2} \pm \frac{\pi}{2} \sin \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\pi}{2} \cos \alpha=\frac{\pi}{2} \pm \frac{\pi}{2} \sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \alpha=1 \pm \sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \alpha \pm \sin \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \alpha+\sin ^{2} \alpha \pm 2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1 \pm \sin 2 \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin 2 \alpha=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \alpha=n \pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \alpha=n \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{n}=0[/math]
 হলে [math]\alpha=0 ;[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{n}=1[/math]
 হলে [math]\alpha=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha=0, \frac{\pi}{2} \quad \text { [Shortcut: Use calculator.] }[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
যদি, [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi[/math] হয় তবে [math]\cot B \cot C+\cot C \cot A+\cot A \cot B[/math] - এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\pi / 2[/math]
B. [math]\pi / 4[/math]
C. [math]1 / 4[/math]
D. [math]1 / 2[/math]
E. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: E.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cot C=\cot \{\pi-(A+B)\} \text { or, }[/math]
 [math]\cot C=-\cot (A+B) \text { or, }[/math]
 [math]\cot C=-\frac{\cot A \cot B-1}{\cot A+\cot B}[/math]
 [math]\text { or, } \cot A \cot C+\cot[/math]
 [math]C \cot B=-\cot A \cot B+1[/math]
 [math]\text { or, }\cot A \cot B+\cot B[/math]
 [math]\cot C+\cot C \cot A=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #451 (ID: 473406)

Question:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]2 \mathrm{n} \pi[/math]
B. [math](2 n \pi+1) \pi[/math]
C. [math]2 n \pi+\pi / 4[/math]
D. [math](2 n-1) \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos[/math]
 [math]\theta+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \theta+\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\sin \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\theta-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]=1=\cos (2 n \pi)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta-\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]=2 n \pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta[/math]
 [math]=2 n \pi+\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]

Question:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}\\\text{Ans: (A) } \frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question #460 (ID: 473418)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]A+B+C=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin \mathrm{B} \cdot \sin \mathrm{C}=-\sin \mathrm{A}[/math] হ্য,তবে [math]\cot A+\cot B+\cot C[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. 1
B. -1
C. 0
D. 2


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cot A+\cot \dot{B}+\cot C=\cot A+\frac{\cos B}{\sin B}+\frac{\cos C}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin C \cdot \cos B+\sin B \cdot \cos C}{\sin B \cdot \sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin (B+C)}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-A\right)}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A-\cot A=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin 2 \alpha[/math]
B. [math]\sin \alpha[/math]
C. [math]\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1-\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}{1+\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\cos 2\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+2 \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 2 \alpha[/math]

Question #462 (ID: 473350)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
