Question #463 (ID: 473351)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019, 2014-2015, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \tan 40^{\circ} \tan 80^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
D. [math]-\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{2 \sin 80^{\circ} \sin 40^{\circ}}{2 \cos 80^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}-\cos 120^{\circ}}{\cos 40^{\circ}+\cos 120^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2}}{\cos 40^{\circ}-\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ}+1}{2 \cos 40^{\circ}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}-\sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ}+\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 60}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #464 (ID: 473352)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board, University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\cot A-\tan A}{\cot A+\tan A}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
D. [math]\cot 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cot A-\tan A}{\cot A+\tan A}=\frac{\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}-\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}}{\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}+\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}} \\=\frac{\cos ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} A}{\cos ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} A}=\cos 2 A\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

 [math]\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{2}[/math]

Question:
[math]\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)+\cos x \sin \left(x+120^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)+\cos x \sin \left(x+120^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos x \sin \left(90^{\circ}+x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos x \cos \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)+\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(x+30^{\circ}-x\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]

Question #471 (ID: 473360)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Sylhet Agricultural University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)+\cos x \sin \left(x+120^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?।

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin x \sin \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)+\cos x \sin \left(x+120^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos x \sin \left(90^{\circ}+x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin x \sin\left(x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(x+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos x+\sin[/math]
 [math]\left(x+30^{\circ}\right) \sin x[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(x+30^{\circ}-x\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]2 \cos \frac{\pi}{13} \cos \frac{9 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]-1[/math]
C. [math]1/2[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}2 \cos \frac{\pi}{13} \cos \frac{9 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13} \\=\cos \frac{10 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{8 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{3 \pi}{13}\right)+\cos \left(\pi-\frac{5 \pi}{13}\right)+\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13} \\=-\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}-\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{3 \pi}{13}+\cos \frac{5 \pi}{13}=0\end{array}[/math]

B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]

D. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

 হলে,[math]\cot A+\cot B+\cot C[/math]
 [math]=\cot 60^{\circ}+\cot 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\cot 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]

Question #474 (ID: 473365)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question #476 (ID: 473367)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের কোণগুলোর অনুপাত [math]1:2:3[/math] হলে, বাহুগুলোর অনুপাত হচ্ছে-

Options:
ক. [math]2: \sqrt{3}: 1[/math]
খ. [math]2: 3: 1[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}: 2: 1[/math]
ঘ. [math]1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]A, 2 A B 3 A[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\mathrm{A}+2 \mathrm{~A}+3 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 6 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]30^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]60^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
 তাহলে, বাহুগুলো [math]a,b,c[/math]
 হলে,[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin 90^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{1}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{b}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] এবং [math]A=\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math] হলে, B=?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{9}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{7 \pi}{18}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5 \pi}{18}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin A-\sin B=\cos B-\cos A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B=\frac{\pi}{2}-A[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5 \pi}{18}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #480 (ID: 473371)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology

Question:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হলে [math]\sin \mathrm{A}-[/math] এর মান হবে?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\text { None of these }[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](b+c+a)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{bc}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #481 (ID: 473372)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{a \cos \varphi-b}{a-b \cos \varphi}[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b} \sin \varphi}{\mathrm{b}-\mathbf{a} \sin \varphi}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{\frac{a+b \cos \varphi}{a-b \sin \varphi}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\frac{a+b}{a-b}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{a}+b}{b}[/math]
E. [math]\frac{(a+b)^{2}}{a-b}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{a \cos \varphi-b}{a-b \cos \varphi}[/math]
 [math]\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}-b}{a-b \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a-a \tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}-b-b \tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}{a+a \tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}-b+b \tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(a-b)-\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)}{(a-b)+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1-\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}-1+\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(a-b)+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)+(a-b)-\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)}{(a-b)+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)-(a-b)+\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2(a-b)}{2 \tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}(a+b)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a+b}{a-b}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\tan \frac{\theta}{2}}{\tan \frac{\varphi}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{a+b}{a-b}}[/math]


Explanation:

 [math]\text { Or, } \cos \left(\theta-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, } \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]=2 n \pi \pm \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, } \theta[/math]
 [math]=2 n \pi, 2 n \pi-\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Question #485 (ID: 473377)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি , [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হয় তবে [math]\operatorname{cosec}(A+B)=[/math] কত

Options:
A. [math]\sec \mathrm{C}[/math]
B. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{C}[/math]
C. [math]\sin C[/math]
D. [math]\cos C[/math]
E. [math]\tan \mathrm{C}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}-C \therefore \operatorname{cosec}(A+B)=\operatorname{cosec}\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-C\right)=\sec C[/math]

Question #494 (ID: 473306)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\cos (A+B) \sin (C+D)[/math] [math]=\cos (A-B) \sin (C-D)[/math] হয় তালে [math]\tan D[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\tan A \tan B \tan C[/math]
B. [math]\cot A \cot B \cot C[/math]
C. [math]\sin A \sin B \sin C[/math]
D. [math]\cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
E. [math]\sec A \sec B \sec C[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos (A+B) \sin (C+D)=\cos (A-B) \sin (C-D)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos (A+B)}{\cos (A-B)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (C-D)}{\sin (C+D)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos (A+B)+\cos (A-B)}{\cos (A+B)-\cos (A-B)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (C-D)+\sin (C+D)}{\sin (C-D)-\sin (C+D)}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos A \cos B}{-\sin A \sin B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin C \cos D}{-\cos C \sin D}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan D[/math]
 [math]=\tan A \tan B \tan C[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

 [math]=\frac{1}{0}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-(\tan A \tan[/math]
 [math]B+\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan A \tan B+\tan[/math]

Question #496 (ID: 473308)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Pabna University of Science and Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C \backsim \cos A=\sin B-\cos C[/math] হলে ত্রিভুজটি হবে-

Options:
A. স্থুলকোণী
B. সমকোণী
C. সূক্ষ্মকোণী
D. কোনটিই নয়


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin (A+C)[/math]
 [math][\because B=\pi-(A+C)][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A+C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{A+C}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A-C=\pi-(A+C)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #505 (ID: 473319)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #506 (ID: 473320)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #508 (ID: 473322)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #509 (ID: 473323)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের কোণগুলোর অনুপাত [math]1:2:3[/math] হলে, বাহুগুলোর অনুপাত হচ্ছে-

Options:
ক. [math]2: \sqrt{3}: 1[/math]
খ. [math]2: 3: 1[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}: 2: 1[/math]
ঘ. [math]1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]A, 2 A B 3 A[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\mathrm{A}+2 \mathrm{~A}+3 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 6 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]30^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]60^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
 তাহলে, বাহুগুলো [math]a,b,c[/math]
 হলে,[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin 90^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{1}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{b}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
যদি [math]\cos 4 \theta=\frac{7}{18}[/math] এবং [math]270^{\circ} \leq 4 \theta \leq 360^{\circ}[/math] তবে [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{5}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{5}{6}[/math]
C. [math]\pm \frac{5}{6}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{11}}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos 4 \theta=\frac{7}{18} \Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} 2 \theta-1=\frac{7}{18}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} 2 \theta=\frac{25}{18} \Rightarrow \cos ^{2} 2 \theta=\frac{25}{36} \Rightarrow \cos 2 \theta= \pm \frac{5}{6} \\\therefore \cos 2 \theta=-\frac{5}{6} \quad\left[\because 135^{\circ} \leq 2 \theta \leq 180^{\circ}\right]\end{array}[/math]

Question #511 (ID: 473325)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)

Question:
[math]\sin \phi+\cos \phi=1[/math] হলে, [math]\sin \phi-\cos \phi[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{-1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\pm 1[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin \phi+\cos \phi=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \phi+\cos ^{2} \phi+2 \sin \phi \cos \phi=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+2 \sin \phi \cos \phi=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \phi \cos \phi=0[/math]
 [math](\sin \phi-\cos \phi)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} \phi+\cos ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\phi-2 \sin \phi \cos \phi[/math]
 [math]=1-0=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \phi-\cos[/math]
 [math]\phi= \pm 1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #512 (ID: 473326)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board, University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\cot A-\tan A}{\cot A+\tan A}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
D. [math]\cot 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cot A-\tan A}{\cot A+\tan A}=\frac{\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}-\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}}{\frac{\cos A}{\sin A}+\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}} \\=\frac{\cos ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} A}{\cos ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} A}=\cos 2 A\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #513 (ID: 473327)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\tan \alpha-\tan \beta=p, \cot \beta-\cot \alpha=q, \alpha-\beta=\theta[/math] তবে [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{p}-\frac{1}{q}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{q}-\frac{1}{p}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
D. [math]1-\frac{p}{q}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]p=\tan \alpha-\tan \beta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}-\frac{\sin \beta}{\cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cdot \cos \beta-\sin \beta \cdot \cos \alpha}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{p}=\frac{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}[/math]
 [math]q=\cot \beta-\cot \alpha=\frac{\cos \beta}{\sin \beta}-\frac{\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cdot \cos \beta-\cos \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}=[/math]
 [math]\cot (\alpha-\beta) ;[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta=\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #514 (ID: 473329)

Question:
[math]A+B+C=(2 n+1) \frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A+\tan A \tan B[/math] এর মান বের কর?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]A+B+C=(2 n+1) \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan (A+B+C)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left\{(2 n+1) \frac{\pi}{2}\right\}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan A+\tan B+\tan C-\tan A+\tan B+\tan C}{1-(\tan A \tan B+\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A)}=\frac{1}{0}=[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-(\tan A \tan B+\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan A \tan B[/math]
 [math]+\tan B \tan C[/math]
 [math]+\tan C \tan A=1[/math]

Question #515 (ID: 473330)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\sin \alpha+\sin \beta=a[/math] এবং [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=b[/math] হয়,

তাহলে, [math]\cos (\alpha-\beta)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}+2}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-2}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}-2}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}+2}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \alpha+\sin \beta=a[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin ^{2} \alpha+\sin ^{2} \beta+2[/math]
 [math]\sin \alpha \sin \beta=a^{2}[/math]
 [math].....(i)[/math]
 [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=b[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\beta+2 \cos \alpha \cos \beta=b^{2}[/math]
 [math]....(ii)[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) }+\text { (ii) } \Rightarrow\left(\sin ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2} \beta\right)+\sin ^{2} {\beta}+\cos ^{2} \beta[/math]
 [math]+2\left(\cos \alpha \cos \beta+\sin \alpha \sin \beta=a^{2}+b^{2}\right.[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2+2 \cos (\alpha-\beta)[/math]
 [math]=a^{2}+b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (u-\beta)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-2}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #516 (ID: 473331)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A এর কোন মানের জন্য [math]\cos A \sin \left(A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান বৃহত্তম হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\text { None of them }[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \left(A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right) \cos A=\frac{1}{2}\left\{2 \cos A \sin \left(A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\right\}=\frac{1}{2}\left\{\sin \left(2 A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)-\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{6}\right)\right\}=\frac{1}{2} \sin \left(2 A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)-\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\text { For maximum value, } \sin \left(2 A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \mathrm{~A}-\frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore 2 \mathrm{~A}=\frac{2 \pi}{3} \therefore \mathrm{A}=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #517 (ID: 473332)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { ABC }[/math] ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রে [math]a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}=2 c^{2}\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math] হলে [math]\cos C[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
খ. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]\pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\text { None of them }[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}[/math]
 [math]=2 c^{2}\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(a^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left(b^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left(-c^{2}\right)^{2}+2 a^{2}\left(-c^{2}\right)+2 b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left(-c^{2}\right)+2 a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\pm \sqrt{2} a b[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b}[/math]
 [math]=\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos C[/math]
 [math]=\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

 [math](\mathrm{i})^{2}+(\mathrm{ii})^{2} ; 1+1+2 \cos (\alpha+\beta)=13 ;[/math]
 [math]\cos (\alpha+\beta)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{11}{2}[/math]
 [math](\mathrm{ii})^{2}-(\mathrm{i})^{2} ;[/math]
 [math]\cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \beta+2 \cos (\alpha-\beta)=5[/math]
 [math]2 \cos (\alpha-\beta)[/math]

Question #523 (ID: 473338)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C \backsim \cos A=\sin B-\cos C[/math] হলে ত্রিভূজটি হবে -

Options:
A. সূক্ষ্মকোণী
B. স্থুলকোণী
C. সমকোণী
D. সমবাহু
E. সমদ্বিবাহু


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]A+B+C=\pi \therefore \frac{A+C}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\cos A=\sin B-\cos C \Rightarrow \cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{(A+C)}{2} \cos \frac{(A-C)}{2}=2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{B}{2}\right) \cos \frac{A-C}{2}-[/math]
 [math]2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}=0[/math]
 [math]2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}-2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}=0 \Rightarrow \cos \frac{A-C}{2}=[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{B}{2} \Rightarrow \frac{A-C}{2}=\frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=B+C[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B+C=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A+A=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #524 (ID: 473339)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin 2 A}{1+\cos 2 A}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\tan 2 A[/math]
B. [math]\tan 3 A[/math]
C. [math]\tan \mathbf{A}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 4 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
E. [math]\tan 5 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin 2 A}{1+\cos 2 A}=\frac{2 \sin A \cdot \cos A}{2 \cos ^{2} A}=\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}=\tan (A)[/math]

Question #525 (ID: 473340)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলো যথাক্রমে [math]3cm, 4cm, 5cm[/math] হলে ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math]6 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
খ. [math]9 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
গ. [math]12 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]10 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]s=\frac{3+4+5}{2}=\frac{12}{2}[/math]
 [math]=6 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \Delta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{6(6-3)(6-4)(6-5)}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{6 \times 3 \times 2 \times 1}[/math]
 [math]=6 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #526 (ID: 473341)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math](1+\tan A)(1+\tan B)=2[/math] হয় তবে [math](A+B)[/math] এর কোন মানটি সত্য?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](1+\tan A)[/math]
 [math]\times(1+\tan B)=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\tan B+[/math]
 [math]\tan A+\tan A[/math]
 [math]\cdot \tan B=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan A+\tan B[/math]
 [math]=1-\tan A \cdot \tan B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \cdot \tan B}[/math]
 [math]=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan (A+B)=[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #529 (ID: 473344)

Question:
[math]\frac{\sin75^{\circ}+\sin15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)=\tan 60^{\circ}=\sqrt{3}\\\text{}\end{array}[/math]

Question #530 (ID: 473345)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #531 (ID: 473346)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 15^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(45^{\circ}- 30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 45^{\circ} \cos[/math]
 [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\cos 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #532 (ID: 473347)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 15^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(45^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}-\cos 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #537 (ID: 473291)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #538 (ID: 473293)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017, 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit A), Chattogram Veterinary and Animal Sciences University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \sin 50^{\circ} \sin 70^{\circ}[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{8}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \sin 50^{\circ} \sin 70^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\left\{\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 120^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sin 10^{\circ}\left(\cos 20^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin 10^{\circ}+\frac{1}{4} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(\sin 30^{\circ}-\sin10^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{4} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #540 (ID: 473296)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর [math]\sin A+\sin B+\sin C=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2 s}{R}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\mathrm{s}}{\mathrm{R}}[/math]
C. [math]0[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{R}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin A+\sin B+\sin C \\=\frac{a}{2 R}+\frac{b}{2 R}+\frac{c}{2 R}=\frac{a+b+c}{2 R}=\frac{2 s}{2 R}=\frac{s}{R}\end{array}[/math]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনো ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]6[/math] বর্গ একক উহার দুই বাহুর দৈঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]3[/math] ও [math]4[/math] একক। তাহলে উক্ত বাহু দুটির অর্ন্তভুক্ত কোণ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
ঘ. কোনোটিই নয়


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{2} \times 3 \times 4 \sin \theta=6 \Rightarrow \sin \theta=1=\sin \frac{\pi}{2} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Question #544 (ID: 473300)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021-2022, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে যদি [math]a=3, b=3 \sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]A=30^{\circ}[/math] হয় তবে B ও C এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]45^{\circ}, 30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]30^{\circ}, 40^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]20^{\circ}, 45^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]10^{\circ}, 70^{\circ}[/math]
ঙ. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: E.[math]30^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{3 \sqrt{3} \times \sin 30^{\circ}}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=60^{\circ} \text { or } 120^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=0^{\circ} \text { or }\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-120^{\circ}-30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \sin 50^{\circ} \sin 70^{\circ}[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{8}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \sin 50^{\circ} \sin 70^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\left\{\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 120^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sin 10^{\circ}\left(\cos 20^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin 10^{\circ}+\frac{1}{4} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(\sin 30^{\circ}-\sin10^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{4} \sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #547 (ID: 473303)

Question:
[math]A B C[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]\angle A=75^{\circ}[/math] এবং [math]\angle B=45^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\mathbf{c}: \mathbf{b}=\text { ? }[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{5}: \sqrt{7}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2}: \sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{3}: \sqrt{2}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}: \sqrt{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\angle C=180^{\circ}-45^{\circ}-75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{c}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{c}{b}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin C}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\sin 45^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\frac{2}{3}}}{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore c: b=\sqrt{3}:[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]

Question #548 (ID: 473304)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Textiles, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\tan \alpha-\tan \beta=p, \cot \beta-\cot \alpha=q, \alpha-\beta=\theta[/math] হয় তবে [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{p}-\frac{1}{q}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{q}-\frac{1}{p}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
D. [math]1-\frac{p}{q}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{p}=\tan \alpha-\tan \beta=\frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}-\frac{\sin \beta}{\cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\sin \beta \cos \alpha}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{p}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}[/math]
 [math]q=\cot \beta-\cot \alpha=\frac{\cos \beta}{\sin \beta}-\frac{\cos \alpha}{\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\cos \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos (\alpha-\beta)}{\sin (\alpha-\beta)}=\cot (\alpha-\beta) ;[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #549 (ID: 473275)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি সমবাহু ত্রিভুজের ভরকেন্দ্রের সাথে যে কোন দুটি কৌণিক বিন্দু সংযুক্ত করে নতুন ত্রিভুজ তৈরি করা হল। নতুন ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল সমবাহু ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফলের কত অংশ হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
ঙ. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

[Image]
Hints: ত্রিভুজের মধ্যমাত্রায় যে বিন্দুতে ছেদ করে তাকে ভরকেন্দ্র বলে। ভরকেন্দ্র মধ্যমাকে 2 : 1 অনুপাতে অন্তঃবিভক্ত করে। সমবাহু ত্রিভুজের মধ্যমা বিপরীত বাহুর ওপর লম্ব হয় ।Solve: মনেকরি, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 সমবাহু,AB = BC = CA = aভরকেন্দ্র GB ও C বিন্দুকে যোগ করে △ BGC গঠন করা হয়েছে; AD মধ্যমাAG: GD = 2:1△ ABC এর ক্ষেত্রফল = [math]\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{BC} \times \mathrm{AD}[/math]
△ AGC এর ক্ষেত্রফল = [math]\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{BC} \times \mathrm{GD}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \frac{\Delta \mathrm{BGC}}{\triangle \mathrm{ABC}}=\frac{\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{BC} \times \mathrm{GD}}{\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{BC} \times \mathrm{AD}}=\frac{\mathrm{GD}}{\mathrm{AD}}=\frac{\mathrm{GD}}{3 \mathrm{GD}}=\frac{1}{3} \\\therefore \triangle \mathrm{BGC}=\frac{1}{3} \times \triangle \mathrm{ABC}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
এখানে AD মধ্যমা G বিন্দুতে 2:1 অনুপাতে অর্ন্তবিভক্ত হয়। ফলে AG:GD = 2:1 ⇒ AG = 2GD = AD - GD = 2GD⇒ AD = 3GD, এই মান AD এর পরিবর্তে বসানো হয়েছে

Question #553 (ID: 473280)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #556 (ID: 473284)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\cos \alpha+\sin \beta=0, \sin \alpha-\cos \beta=1[/math] এবং [math]90^{\circ} \leq\{\alpha, \beta\} \leq 180^{\circ}[/math] হয়, তবে [math](\alpha-\beta)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]75^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math](\cos \alpha+\sin \beta)^{2}+(\sin \alpha-\cos \beta)^{2}=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+1+2 \cos \alpha \sin \beta-2 \sin \alpha \cos \beta=1 \\\Rightarrow(\sin \alpha \cos \beta-\cos \alpha \sin \beta)=\frac{1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin (\alpha-\beta)=\sin 30^{\circ} \therefore \alpha-\beta=30^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #558 (ID: 473286)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011, 2022-2023, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #561 (ID: 473268)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A B C[/math] ত্রিভূজে যদি [math]a=3, b=3 \sqrt{3}[/math] এবং [math]A=30^{\circ}[/math] হয় তবে [math]B[/math] ও [math]C[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]45^{\circ}, 30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]30^{\circ}, 40^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]20^{\circ}, 45^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]30^{\circ}, 90^{\circ}[/math]
ঙ. [math]10^{\circ}, 70^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{a}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B=\sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{b \sin A}{a}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{3 \sqrt{3} \times \sin 30^{\circ}}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=180^{\circ}-(A+B)[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-\left(30^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=90^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #562 (ID: 473269)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin x}{\sin y}=\sqrt{2}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\tan x}{\tan y}=\sqrt{3}[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এবং [math]y[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4} \cdot \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3} \cdot \frac{\pi}{5}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{\pi}{3},-\frac{\pi}{8}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{7} \cdot \frac{\pi}{5}[/math]
E. [math]-\pi, \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan x}{\tan y}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sin x}{\sin y}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}\left(\frac{\cos x}{\cos y}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos x}{\cos y}=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} x}{\cos ^{2} y}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} x[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos ^{2} y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3-3 \sin ^{2} x[/math]
 [math]=2-2 \sin ^{2} y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \sin ^{2} x-2 \sin ^{2} y=1[/math]
 [math]....(i)[/math]
আবার, [math]\frac{\sin x}{\sin y}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} x-2 \sin ^{2} y=0[/math]
 [math].....(ii)[/math]
 [math](i)[/math]
 ও [math](ii)[/math]
 সমাধান করে পাই, [math]x=\frac{\pi}{4},[/math]
 [math]y=\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{1}{\sin 10^{\circ}}-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\operatorname{cos} 10^{\circ}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]4[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]3[/math]
D. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{2}{\sin 10^{\circ}}-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\cos 10^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos 10^{\circ}-\sqrt{5} \sin 10^{\circ}}{\sin 10^{\circ} \cos 10^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4\left(\sin 10^{\circ} \cos 10^{\circ}-\cos 30^{\circ} \sin 10^{\circ}\right)}{2 \sin 10^{\circ} \cos 10^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4 \sin 20^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=4[/math]


Explanation:

Question #566 (ID: 473273)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি সমদ্বিবাহু ত্রিভুজের অসম বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য ও পরিব্যাসার্ধ যথাক্রমে ৪ ও 5 একক। পরিকেন্দ্রটি ত্রিভূজের অভ্যন্তরে হলে সমবাহুদ্বয়ের প্রত্যেকটির দৈর্ঘ্য কত একক?

Options:
ক. [math]4 \sqrt{2}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{5}[/math]
গ. [math]4 \sqrt{5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
ঙ. [math]3 \sqrt{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Hints: Sine Rule: } \frac{a}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]

[Image]
Solve:পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ, R = 5[math]\frac{b}{\sin B}=2 R \Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{b}{2 R}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B=\sin ^{-1} \frac{8}{10} \approx 53^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle B+\angle A+\angle C[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \angle A+\angle C[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-\angle B=127^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle A=\angle C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{127^{\circ}}{2}=63.5^{\circ}[/math]
এবং [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a=2 R \sin A=2 \times 5 \times \sin 63.5^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=8.94=4 \sqrt{5}[/math]


Explanation:
উক্ত Problem এ সমদ্বিবাহু ত্রিভুজের বেসিক কনসেপ্ট এবং sin এর সূত্র ব্যবহার করে করা হয়েছে। মনে রাখবে, সমদ্বিবাহু ত্রিভুজের সমান সমান বাহুর বিপরীত কোণগুলোও সমান হয়।

Question:
[math]\sin 54^{\circ}=\frac{1}{4}(1+\sqrt{5})[/math] হলে [math]\cos 36^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত ?

B. [math]\frac{1}{4}(1-\sqrt{5})[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{4}(-1-\sqrt{5})[/math]
E. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\pm \sqrt{5} \pm 1)[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Hints: [math]\sin \theta=\cos (90-\theta)[/math]
Solve:, [math]\sin \theta=\cos (90-\theta)[/math]
যেমন, [math]\sin 30^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 তেমনি [math]\cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
যেহেতু, দেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin 54^{0}=\frac{1}{4}(1+\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math](90-54)=36[/math]
 ;[math]\cos 36^{0}=\sin 54^{0}=\frac{1}{4}(1+\sqrt{5})[/math]

Question:

B. [math]\tan 10^{\circ}[/math]

D. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

 [math]=\tan 40^{\circ} \tan \left(90^{\circ}-40^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cot 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]

Question #569 (ID: 473257)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014, 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]9, 40[/math] ও [math]41[/math] একক বাহুবিশিষ্ট একটি ত্রিভুজের পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস কত?

Options:
ক. [math]41[/math]
খ. [math]21.5[/math]
গ. [math]20.5[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{9 \times 40 \times 41}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]s=\frac{9+40+41}{2}=45[/math]
 [math]\therefore \Delta=\sqrt{45(45-9)(45-40)(45-41)}=180[/math]
পরিবৃত্তের ব্যাস, [math]=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]=2 \times \frac{\mathrm{abc}}{4 \Delta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{abc}}{2 \Delta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \times 40 \times 41}{2 \times 180}[/math]
 [math]=41[/math]
 এককপরিবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ, [math]R=20.5[/math]


Explanation:

Question #570 (ID: 473259)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]2 \cos \frac{\pi}{16}=?[/math]

Options:

B. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]

 [math]=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2 \frac{\pi}{8}}}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]

Question:
[math]\cos ^{2} \mathbf{A}+\cos ^{2}\left(\mathbf{A}+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)+\cos ^{2}\left(\mathbf{A}-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math] এর মান কোনটি-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3}{2}+1[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}+5[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{7}[/math]
E. [math]\frac{7}{9}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\cos ^{2}\left(\mathrm{~A}+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2}\left(\mathrm{~A}-\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left\{1+\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+1+\cos \left(2 \mathrm{~A}+\frac{2 \pi}{3}\right)+1+\cos \left(2 \mathrm{~A}-\frac{2 \pi}{3}\right)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(3+\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+2 \cos 2 \mathrm{~A} \cos \frac{2 \pi}{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left\{3+\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+2 \cos 2 \mathrm{~A}\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)\right\}=\frac{3}{2}[/math]

Question:
[math]\triangle \mathbf{A B C}[/math] এ [math]b=7.8, c=8.6, A=45^{\circ}[/math] হলে, ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল কোনটি?

ক. [math]23[/math]
খ. [math]23.7[/math]

ঘ. [math]27[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} b c \sin A=\frac{1}{2} \times 7.8 \times 8.6 \times \sin 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 7.8 \times 8.6 \times \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=23.7[/math]
 বর্গএকক।

Question #576 (ID: 473266)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের কোণগুলোর অনুপাত [math]1:2:3[/math] হলে, বাহুগুলোর অনুপাত হচ্ছে-

Options:
ক. [math]2: \sqrt{3}: 1[/math]
খ. [math]2: 3: 1[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}: 2: 1[/math]
ঘ. [math]1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]A, 2 A B 3 A[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\mathrm{A}+2 \mathrm{~A}+3 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 6 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 কোণগুলো [math]30^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]60^{\circ},[/math]
 [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
 তাহলে, বাহুগুলো [math]a,b,c[/math]
 হলে,[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin 90^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{a}}{1}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{b}:[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=1: \sqrt{3}: 2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] হলে [math]\sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)=[/math] কত ?

A. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)=\sin ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}=1-\frac{1}{4}-\frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]

Question:
[math]\cos \left(150^{\circ}-\theta\right)=\frac{1}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]90°[/math]
B. [math]75°[/math]
C. $ 45° $
D. [math]30°[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}\cos \left(150^{\circ}-\theta\right) & =\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow 150^{\circ}-\theta & =60 \therefore \theta=90^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #581 (ID: 473248)

Question:
[math]\frac{\tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\tan 2 \theta[/math]
B. [math]\sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
C. [math]2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=\sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]

Question #582 (ID: 473249)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}+\frac{1-\cos A}{\sin A}[/math] এর মান হচ্ছে-

Options:
A. [math]2 \operatorname{cosec} A[/math]
B. [math]2 \tan \frac{A}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \cot A[/math]
D. [math]2 \sec A[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}+\frac{1-\cos A}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin ^{2} A+1-\cos ^{2} A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin ^{2} A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sin A}{1+\cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cdot 2 \sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}}{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=2 \tan \frac{A}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #583 (ID: 473250)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A ও B ধনাত্মক সূক্ষ্মকোণ এবং [math]\sin A=\frac{3}{5}, \cos B=\frac{12}{13}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos (\mathbf{A}+\mathbf{B})[/math]এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{15}{65}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{33}{65}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{18}{65}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{65}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

[Image]
[math]\sin A=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
আবার, [math]\cos B=\frac{12}{13}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{5}{13}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (A+B)=[/math]
 [math]\cos A \cos B-\sin A \sin B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4}{5} \cdot \frac{12}{13}-\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{5}{13}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{48-15}{5.13}=\frac{33}{65}[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\cos 18^{\circ}+\cos 162^{\circ}+\cos 234^{\circ}+\cos 1386^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]-1[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

 [math]=\cos 18^{\circ}+\cos \left(180^{\circ}-18^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos \left(180^{\circ}+54^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\cos \left(4 \times 360^{\circ}-54^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\cos 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\cos 54^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\cos 54^{\circ}=0[/math]

Question:
[math]2 \cos \frac{\pi}{16}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}}=\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{8}\right)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{4 \cos \frac{2 \pi}{8}}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}} \\=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}\end{array}[/math]

Question #587 (ID: 473254)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #588 (ID: 473255)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos 75^{\circ}=\cos[/math]
 [math]\left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
