Question #592 (ID: 473235)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011, 2022-2023, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin A[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\tan \mathrm{A}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)[/math]
 [math]=\tan[/math]
 [math]A\left(1+\frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \mathrm{A}\left(\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+1+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \mathrm{A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]

Question #594 (ID: 473237)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019, 2014-2015, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \tan 40^{\circ} \tan 80^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
D. [math]-\sqrt{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{2 \sin 80^{\circ} \sin 40^{\circ}}{2 \cos 80^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}-\cos 120^{\circ}}{\cos 40^{\circ}+\cos 120^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2}}{\cos 40^{\circ}-\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ}+1}{2 \cos 40^{\circ}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}-\sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ}+\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 60}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\tan x[/math]
B. [math]\cos x[/math]
C. [math]\sec x[/math]
D. [math]\sin x[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2 x)}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2 \times 2 \cos ^{2} 2 x}}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+2 \cos 2 x}} \\=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2 x)}}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} x}}=\frac{2}{2 \cos x}=\sec x\end{array}[/math]

 [math]=\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{12}=75^{\circ}[/math]

Question #599 (ID: 473224)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University of Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { In the following figure, the curse } \mathrm{C} \text { has the parametric cquations- }[/math] [math]x=4 \cos \left(t+\frac{\pi}{6}\right), y=2 \sin t, 0 \leq t \leq 2 \pi ; \text { Find } x+y[/math]


[Image]


Options:
A. [math]1 \sqrt{3} \sin t[/math]
B. [math]2 \sqrt{3} \cos t[/math]
C. [math]2 \sqrt{3} \sin t[/math]
D. [math]1 \sqrt{3} \cos t[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]x=4 \cos \left(t+\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math]
 [math]=4 \cos t \cos \frac{\pi}{6}-4[/math]
 [math]\sin t \sin \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sqrt{3} \cos t-2 \sin t[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow2 \sqrt{3} \cos t-y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x + y=2 \sqrt{3} \text { cost. }[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{y}{x}[/math] হলে [math]x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]y[/math]
B. [math]y^{2} / x^{2}[/math]
C. [math]x[/math]
D. [math]x^{2} / y^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x \times \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]+y \times \frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=x\left(\frac{1-\frac{y^{2}}{x^{2}}}{1+\frac{y^{2}}{x^{2}}}\right)[/math]
 [math]+y\left(\frac{2 \times \frac{y}{x}}{1+\frac{x^{2}}{y^{2}}}\right)=x[/math]


Explanation:

Question #602 (ID: 473227)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]k{, l}[/math] -এর কোন মানের জন্য [math]5 \sin (k \theta)=(10 l+9) \sin \theta+(15 l+6) \cos \theta[/math]

Options:
A. [math]-1,-\frac{2}{5}[/math]
B. [math]1,-\frac{2}{5}[/math]
C. [math]1,-\frac{5}{2}[/math]
D. [math]-1, \frac{2}{5}[/math]
E. [math]2, \frac{5}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: চলকের যে কোনো মানের জন্য যখন কোনো সমীকরণের বামপক্ষ ও ডানপক্ষ সমান হয় তখন সেই সমীকরণকে অভেদ বলে।Solve : [দ্রুত করার জন্য Calculator এর মাধ্যমে Solve করো][math]\theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 ধরে নিয়ে, (C) অপশন থেকে,[ θ এর অন্য যেকোন মান ধরলে হবে ]k = 1 এবং [math]1=-\frac{2}{5}[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { L.H.S }=5 \sin (k \theta)=5 \sin (1.30)=\frac{5}{2} \\\text { R.H.S }=(10 l+9) \sin \theta+(15 l+6) \cos \theta \\=\left(10 \frac{-2}{5}+9\right) \sin 30+\left(15 \frac{-2}{5}+6\right) \cos 30=\frac{5}{2}\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ k = 1 এবং [math]1=-\frac{2}{5}[/math]
 হলে θ এর যেকোনো মানের জন্যই সমীকরণটির বামপক্ষ আর ডানপক্ষ সমান।

Explanation:
একটি সমীকরণকে তখনই অভেন বলা হবে যখন চলকের যে কোনো মানের জন্য সমীকরণের উভয়পক্ষ সমান হবে। যেমন [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=1-\cos ^{2} \theta[/math] একটি অভেদ। কারণ θ এর যেকোনো মানের জন্য সমীকরণটির বামপক্ষ ও তানপক্ষের মান সমান। মনে রাখবে, সকল অভেদই সমীকরণ কিন্তু সকল সমীকরণ অভেদ নয়।

Question #604 (ID: 473229)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে [math]\sin (B+C)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{A+C}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{B}{2} \cos \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{A-C}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A[/math]
 [math]=B+C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=180^{\circ}-\Lambda[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin (B+C)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 90^{\circ}=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #605 (ID: 473231)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #606 (ID: 473223)

Question:
[math]\text { In } \triangle A B C, a=2 b \text { and } \angle A=3 \theta, \text { what is the value of } \theta \text { ? }[/math]


[Image]


Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Applying sine rule we get, }[/math]
 [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 b}{\sin 3\theta}=\frac{b}{\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \theta=\sin 3 \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2=3-4 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta=30^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #608 (ID: 473220)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2014-2015, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin 2 \alpha[/math]
B. [math]\sin \alpha[/math]
C. [math]\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)-1}{\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)+1}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1-\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}{1+\tan ^{2}\left(\alpha+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\cos 2\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+2 \alpha\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin 2 \alpha[/math]


Explanation:

Question #609 (ID: 473221)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (A Unit, Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Sylhet Agricultural University, Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]a: b: c=3: 7: 5[/math] হলে [math]\angle B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a=3 \mathrm{k}, \mathrm{b}=7 \mathrm{k},[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{c}=5 \mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ac}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{9 \mathrm{k}^{2}+25 \mathrm{k}^{2}-49 \mathrm{k}^{2}}{2 \times 3 \times 5 \mathrm{k}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{34-49}{30}=\frac{-15}{30}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{3}-2[/math]
খ. [math]2-\sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]1+\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3-\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan 15^{\circ}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\tan 30^{\circ}}{1+\tan 30^{\circ}}=\frac{1-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}{1+1 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}=2-\sqrt{3}[/math]

Question #612 (ID: 473213)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangamata Sheikh Fojilatunnesa Mujib Science and Technology University

Question:
[math]\cos 15^{\circ}[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{3}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{3}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \sqrt{2 \cos ^{2} 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{1+\cos 2 \times 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{1+\cos 30^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{1+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Explanation:

 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Question #615 (ID: 473216)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\sin 18^{\circ}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)[/math] তবে [math]\cos 36^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}+1)[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{5}(\sqrt{4}-1)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{5}(\sqrt{4}+1)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 36^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2.18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1-2 \sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1-2\left\{\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)\right\}^{2}[/math]
 [math]=1-2\left\{\frac{1}{16}(5+1-2 \sqrt{5})\right\}[/math]
 [math]=1-\frac{1}{8}(6-2 \sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=1-\frac{1}{4}(3-\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(4-3+\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(1+\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}+1)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #617 (ID: 473218)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019-2020, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board, Rajshahi University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]0^{\circ}<\theta<180^{\circ}[/math], তবে [math]\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{\ldots+2(1+\cos \theta)}}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]2 \cos \frac{0}{2^{n-1}}[/math]
B. [math]2 \cos \frac{\theta}{2^{n+1}}[/math]
C. [math]2 \cos \frac{\theta}{2^{n}}[/math]
D. [math]2 \cos \frac{n \theta}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin \delta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin (\theta+\delta) \cdot \sin (\theta-\delta)=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ} \therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin \delta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\sin 45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \delta=45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \left(60^{\circ}+45^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\sin \left(60^{\circ}-45^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 60^{\circ}-\sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{4}-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3-2}{4}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #619 (ID: 473185)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2020-2021, 2018-2019, 2009-2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit)

Question:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin A[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\tan \mathrm{A}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)[/math]
 [math]=\tan[/math]
 [math]A\left(1+\frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \mathrm{A}\left(\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+1+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \mathrm{A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #620 (ID: 473186)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Khulna University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

 [math]\left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]-\sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

Question #624 (ID: 473190)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011, 2022-2023, 2018-2019, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math](a+b+c)[/math] [math](b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হয় তবে A কোণের মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]50^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]40^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}+2 b c-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A[/math]
 [math]=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan A(1+\sec 2 A)=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin A[/math]
B. [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
C. [math]\tan \mathrm{A}[/math]
D. [math]\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

 [math]=\tan[/math]
 [math]A\left(1+\frac{1+\tan ^{2} A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \mathrm{A}\left(\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+1+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \tan \mathrm{A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]

Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math] বর্গ সে.মি. এবং উহার দুই বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]3[/math] সে.মি. এবং [math]5[/math] সে.মি. উক্ত বাহু দুইটির অন্তর্গত কোণ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]30^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]135^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\Delta=\frac{1}{2} a b \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{15 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 3[/math]
 [math]\times 5 \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\sin 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]

 [math]=2 \cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\left(-\sin 10^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\left(-\sin 10^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=-\sin 10^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin 10^{\circ}=0[/math]

 [math]\tan (A+B)[/math]

 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math](1-\tan A \tan B)+\tan A \tan B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+1-\tan A \tan[/math]
 [math]B+\tan A \tan B=2[/math]

Question #632 (ID: 473200)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos 20 \cos 40 \cos 60 \cos 80=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{8}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{12}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{16}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos 20^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 60^{\circ} \cos 80^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 80^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\times \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4} \cdot\left(2 \cos 80^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(\cos 120^{\circ}+\cos 40^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(-\frac{1}{2}+\cos 40^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(-\frac{1}{2} \cos 20^{\circ}+\cos 40^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left(-\frac{1}{2} \cos 20^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2} \cos 60^{\circ}+\frac{1}{2} \cos 20^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8} \cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{8}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{16}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #635 (ID: 473203)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A}+\mathbf{B}+\mathbf{C}=\pi[/math] হলে, [math]\cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]1+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
B. [math]1+\cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
C. [math]1-\cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
D. [math]1-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]A=B=C=60^{\circ}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\cos ^{2} 60^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 60^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}+\frac{1}{4}+\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\text { Option D }[/math]
হতে পাই, [math]1-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
 [math]=1-2 \times \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3}{4}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
কোনো ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রে [math]2 s=a+b+c[/math] হলে, [math]b \cos \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}+\operatorname{accos} \frac{B}{2}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]a b \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\text { abc } \cos ^{2} \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]s^{2}-a b \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math]
D. [math]s-a b \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]b c \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}+a c \cos ^{2} \frac{B}{2}+a b \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}=s^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b c \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}+a c \cos ^{2} \frac{B}{2}=s^{2}-a b \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #637 (ID: 473205)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
[math]ABC[/math] যে কোন ত্রিভুজ হলে, [math]\frac{1}{a} \sin A+\frac{1}{b} \sin B+\frac{1}{c} \sin C=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{6 \Delta}{a b c}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4 \Delta}{a^{2} b^{2} c^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\Delta}{a b c}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4 \Delta}{2 a b}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{a} \sin A+\frac{1}{b} \sin B+\frac{1}{c} \sin C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{a} \times \frac{2 \Delta}{b c}+\frac{1}{b} \times \frac{2 \Delta}{c a}+\frac{1}{c} \times \frac{2 \Delta}{b a}=\frac{6 \Delta}{a b c}[/math]


Explanation:

 [math]30^{\circ}[/math]

 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]

Question #641 (ID: 473210)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2004-2005, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2018-2019, 2017-2018, 2016-2017, 2016-2017, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2013-2014, 2011-2012, 2008-2009, 2001-2002 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Jessore University of Science & Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Mymensingh Board, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{A B C}[/math] ত্রিভুজের [math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\because \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi=2 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #642 (ID: 473211)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

 [math]+\tan 168^{\circ}+\tan 12^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 198^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin \left\{7 \times 90^{\circ}-198^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan \left\{180^{\circ}-12^{\circ}\right\}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 198^{\circ}-\cos 198^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 12^{\circ}-\tan 12=0[/math]

Question:
[math]\tan^{-1}\left(\frac{1}{3}\right) + \frac{1}{2}\tan^{-1}\left(\frac{1}{7}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\tan^{-1}\left(\frac{13}{16}\right)[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2}\tan^{-1}\left(\frac{13}{16}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

, তবে এখানে একটি অর্ধেক আছে।আনুমানিকভাবে এটি [math]1.57[/math]
 রেডিয়ান, যা [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 এর সমান।

Question #646 (ID: 473167)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan\frac{\theta}{2} = \frac{3}{4}[/math] হলে [math]\cos\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{9}{25}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{24}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{25}{7}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos\theta = \frac{1 - \tan^2(\theta/2)}{1 + \tan^2(\theta/2)} = \frac{1 - (9/16)}{1 + (9/16)} = \frac{7/16}{25/16} = \frac{7}{25}[/math]

Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2024-2025 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (B Unit)

Question:
[math]\sin(A - 30^\circ) + \sin(150^\circ + A) =[/math] ?

Options:
A. [math]\cos A[/math]
B. [math]\sin A[/math]
C. [math]\sin A + \cos A[/math]
D. [math]\sin A \cos A[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সূত্র ব্যবহার করি: [math]\sin(A - B) + \sin(A + B) = 2\sin A \cos B[/math]
। এখানে [math]B = 30^\circ[/math]
 এবং [math]B = 150^\circ[/math]
 হলে [math]\cos 30^\circ = \cos 150^\circ[/math]
, কিন্তু একটির মান ধনাত্মক, অন্যটির ঋণাত্মক। ফলাফলসংক্রান্ত বিশ্লেষণ করলে দেখা যায়, সম্পূর্ণ রাশি শেষ পর্যন্ত [math]\sin A[/math]
 এর সমান হয়।

Question #648 (ID: 473169)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]A+B+C=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin \mathrm{B} \cdot \sin \mathrm{C}=-\sin \mathrm{A}[/math] হ্য,তবে [math]\cot A+\cot B+\cot C[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. 1
B. -1
C. 0
D. 2


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cot A+\cot \dot{B}+\cot C=\cot A+\frac{\cos B}{\sin B}+\frac{\cos C}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin C \cdot \cos B+\sin B \cdot \cos C}{\sin B \cdot \sin C}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin (B+C)}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A+\frac{\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-A\right)}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cot A-\cot A=0[/math]


Explanation:

[math]8 \sin \frac{4 \theta}{2}-8 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1[/math] এর মান কোনটি ?

B. [math]2 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]

 [math]=-8 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2} \cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1=-2.4 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2} \cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1=1-2 \sin ^{2} \theta \\= cos2\theta[/math]

Question #650 (ID: 473171)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2^{4}}\right)[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2^{4}}\right)=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2 \cdot 2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2\left(1-\cos \frac{\pi}{8}\right)}=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-2 \cos \frac{\pi}{8}} \\=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2}\frac{\pi}{8}}}=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2 \sqrt{2+2 \times \frac{1}{\sqrt2}}}= \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #651 (ID: 473172)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]sin4\theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{25}{24}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{24}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{9}{10}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin 4 \theta=\sin 2.2 \theta=2 \sin 2 \theta \cos 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=2 \times \frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta} \times \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=2 \times \frac{2 \times \frac{1}{3}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}} \times \frac{1-\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}}=\frac{24}{25}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #655 (ID: 473176)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{5}{12}\left(\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}\right)[/math] হলে [math]\sin (-\theta)+\cos \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{5}{13}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{7}{13}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{7}{13}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

[Image]
[math]\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে,[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \theta=-\frac{5}{13} \\\cos \theta=-\frac{12}{13}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\sin (-\theta)+\cos \theta=-\sin \theta+\cos \theta=\frac{5}{13}-\frac{12}{13}=\frac{-7}{13}[/math]


Explanation:

B. 1
C. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]

Question #657 (ID: 473180)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit C)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\sin \frac{A}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\cos \frac{A}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\cot \frac{A}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\tan \frac{\mathrm{A}}{2}[/math]
E. [math]\text { none of these }[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}=\frac{2 \sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}}{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{A}{2}}=\tan \frac{A}{2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #658 (ID: 473181)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]8 \sin ^{4} \frac{\theta}{2}-8 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]2 \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
B. [math]2 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]8 \sin ^{4} \frac{\theta}{2}-8 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1[/math]
 [math]=2\left(2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]-4[/math]
 [math]\times 2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+1[/math]
 [math]=2(1-\cos \theta)^{2}[/math]
 [math]-4(1-\cos \theta)+1[/math]
 [math]=2\left(1-2 \cos \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta\right)[/math]
 [math]-4+4 \cos \theta+1[/math]
 [math]=2-4 \cos \theta+2[/math]
 [math]\cos ^{2} \theta-4+4[/math]
 [math]\cos \theta+1=2[/math]
 [math]\cos ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #659 (ID: 473182)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=m \cos \theta[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=n \cos \theta[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\left(m^{2}-n^{2}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]4 \mathrm{mn}[/math]
B. [math]4 \sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{\mathrm{mn}}[/math]
D. [math]\mathrm{mn}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta+\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=m \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\sin \theta \cos \theta=m \cos \theta \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta+\sin \theta=m\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]m^{2}-n^{2}=(m+n)(m-n)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=4 \tan \theta \sin \theta=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right)} \\=4 \sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta}=4 \sqrt{m n}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \theta-\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta=n \cos \theta \\\therefore \tan \theta-\sin \theta=n \\m+n=2 \tan \theta \\m-n=2 \sin \theta \\m n=\tan ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #660 (ID: 473183)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{x}[/math], হলে [math]\sin 2 \theta=[/math] কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2 x}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1-x^{2}}{1+x^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1+x^{2}}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{2 x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin 2 \theta=\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{2 \cdot \frac{1}{x}}{1+\frac{1}{x^{2}}}=\frac{2 x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #661 (ID: 473162)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018, 2023-2024 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Rajshahi (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. sin (A - B)
B. sin(B - A)
C. cos(B - A)
D. -cos(A-B)


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
$\begin{array}{l}=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B)=-\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \sin (A-B) \\=-\sin (A-B)=\sin (B-A)\end{array}$[math]\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}[/math]
 [math]=-\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (B+A) \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-[/math]
 [math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}\right) \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]=-\sin (A-B)=\sin (B-A)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #662 (ID: 473163)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016, 2013-2014, 2023-2024, 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020, 2019-2020, 2017-2018, 2015-2016, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2014-2015, 2012-2013, 2011-2012, 2011-2012, 2000-2001 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Jahangirnagar University (C Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit), Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit), Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] হলে, [math]A+B=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\pi[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
C. [math]2 \pi[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \mathrm{A}-\sin \mathrm{B}=\cos \mathrm{B}-\cos \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2} \therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Explanation:

Question #711 (ID: 473518)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos ^{2} 0^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 10^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\ldots . .+\cos ^{2} 90^{\circ}[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]6[/math]
B. [math]3[/math]
C. [math]5[/math]
D. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
পদ [math]=\frac{90-0}{10}+1[/math]
 [math]=10[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 মান = [math]=\frac{10}{2}[/math]
 [math]=5[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #712 (ID: 473519)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin A+\cos A=\sin B+\cos B[/math] এবং [math]A=\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math] হলে, B=?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{9}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{7 \pi}{18}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5 \pi}{18}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin A-\sin B[/math]
 [math]=\cos B-\cos A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}=2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{A+B}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B=\frac{\pi}{2}-A[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5 \pi}{18}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #713 (ID: 473520)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi[/math] এবং [math]\sin \theta=\frac{5}{13}[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}[/math] এর মান

Options:
A. [math]\frac{3}{10}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2}{13}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{\tan \theta+\sec (-\theta)}{\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)}=\frac{\tan \theta+\sec \theta}{\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{-5}{12}-\frac{13}{12}}{\frac{-12}{5}-\frac{13}{5}}=\frac{3}{10}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:
